Bloom is your all-in-one trading solution, built for speed, simplicity, and seamless performance, perfect whether you're just starting out or already a seasoned trader.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/#supported-blockchains)

Supported Blockchains:

**🟪 Solana ⬜️ Ethereum 🟨 BSC 🟦 Base 🟩 HyperEVM 🟪 Monad**

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/#why-bloom)

Why Bloom

*   **Insanely Fast Fills**: Trade faster than ever with our optimized and fully rebuilt infrastructure.
    
*   **Hybrid Trading**: Combine advanced web-based extension settings and powerful Telegram tools for unmatched flexibility.
    
*   **Trade Anywhere, Anytime**: Seamlessly switch from desktop to mobile trading through our user-friendly Telegram bot.
    

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/#core-features)

Core Features

*   **Spot Buy & Sell:** Instant trading made easy.
    
*   **Sniper:** Quickly catch new token opportunities.
    
*   **Copy-Trading:** Effortlessly copy successful traders in real-time.
    
*   **AFK Mode:** Automate your trading even when you're away.
    
*   **Chrome Extension:** Supercharge your trading terminal with advanced tools.
    
*   **Multiple Limit Orders:** Execute your strategies with precision.
    
*   **In-Bot Bridge:** Conveniently bridge tokens between blockchains within the bot.
    
*   **Advanced Settings:** Fully customize your trading experience to your style.
    

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/#supercharged-extension)

Supercharged Extension

Our Chrome Extension boosts your trading terminal with:

*   Faster trades
    
*   Rich customization
    
*   Easy wallet integration
    
*   Enhanced notifications
    

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/#rewards-and-benefits)

Rewards & Benefits

Enjoy fee discounts and an attractive referral program, increasing your earnings while trading.

[NextCashback](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/cashback)

# Cashback | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

Welcome to Bloom Bot’s Cashback Program! We’re excited to offer you a simple and rewarding way to earn back a portion of your trading fees while using Bloom.

With every trade you make, you’ll generate cashback based on your trading volume. Your cashback accumulates directly in the Referral Menu, where you’ll also find your referral rewards. Every 6 hours, you’ll have the chance to claim both cashback and referral fees together with a single click, as long as your balance is above the tresholds.

The more you trade, the more cashback you earn, and if you’re a Bloom Partner, your percentage can be even higher, unlocking even greater rewards.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/cashback#id-10-referred-cashback)

**10% Referred Cashback**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you join Bloom through a referral link, you’ll automatically unlock a 10% cashback on our standard trading fees. Every trade you make generates cashback based on your trading volume, and your rewards are visible at all times inside the Referral Menu.

**How to get your 10% Cashback**[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/cashback#how-to-get-your-10-cashback)

1.  Sign up through a referral link.
    
2.  Start trading and automatically benefit from a 10% cashback on your trading volume.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/cashback#payouts)

Payouts


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cashback and referral fees are available for claim every 6 hours. To process a claim, your unclaimed balance must exceed the tresholds.

If your balance is below this threshold, you’ll simply need to wait until it accumulates above the minimum before claiming.

Blockchain

Minimum Amount Needed

SOL

0.1 SOL

ETH

0.01 ETH

BASE

0.01 ETH

BSC

0.05 BNB

HYPEREVM

1 HYPE

PLASMA

50 XPL

MONAD

1000 MON

# Referrals | Bloom

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3158159183-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAZVSZEL47N9f4qOtz3Wz%252Fuploads%252FoDX6yxkIRYFWZdCl77wI%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8783334a-d552-4c8e-bdf8-aaf9e1773a1d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=df423cc7&sv=2)

Welcome to Bloom Bot’s Revenue Share Program! We’re excited to offer you an opportunity to earn passive income by referring others to our platform. Our program is designed to reward you at multiple levels, maximizing your earning potential as you help grow the Bloom Bot community.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/referrals#referral-link)

**Referral Link**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you join Bloom, you’ll receive a **unique referral link**. Share this link with others, and whenever someone signs up through your link and starts trading, you’ll begin to earn a percentage of the fees they generate on every buy and sell transaction.

The higher their traded volume is, the more you earn! Exponentially.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/referrals#revenue-share-breakdown)

**Revenue Share Breakdown**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Our revenue share program operates on a **3-level system**:

1\. Level 1 – Earn 25% commission

2\. Level 2 – Earn 3% commission

3\. Level 3 – Earn 2% commission

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/referrals#level-1-direct-referrals-25)

**Level 1: Direct Referrals (25%)**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Who counts as Level 1? Anyone who signs up using your unique referral link.
    
*   Your Earnings – You earn 25% of Bloom Bot’s 1% fee on every trade made by your Level 1 referrals.
    

Example[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/referrals#example)

1.  `You (Person A) share your referral link with a friend, Person B.`
    
2.  `Person B signs up using your link and trades $10,000 in a day.`
    
3.  `Bloom Bot’s Fee: $10,000 * 1% = $100`
    
4.  `Your Commission: 25% of $100 = $25`
    

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/referrals#level-2-indirect-referrals-3)

**Level 2: Indirect Referrals (3%)**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Who counts as Level 2? Users who sign up using your Level 1 referrals’ links.
    
*   Your Earnings – You earn 3% of Bloom Bot’s 1% fee on every trade made by your Level 2 referrals.
    

Example[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/referrals#example-1)

1.  `Person B shares their referral link with Person C.`
    
2.  `Person C signs up and trades $10,000 in a day.`
    
3.  `Bloom Bot’s Fee: $10,000 * 1% = $100`
    
4.  `Your Commission: 3% of $100 = $3`
    
5.  `Person B’s Commission: 25% of $100 = $25`
    

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/referrals#level-3-extended-referrals-2)

**Level 3: Extended Referrals (2%)**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Who counts as Level 3? Users who sign up using your Level 2 referrals’ links.
    
*   Your Earnings – You earn 2% of Bloom Bot’s 1% fee on every trade made by your Level 3 referrals.
    

Example[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/referrals#example-2)

1.  `Person C shares their referral link with Person D`
    
2.  `Person D signs up and trades $10,000 in a day.`
    
3.  `Bloom Bot’s Fee: $10,000 * 1% = $100`
    
4.  `Your Commission: 2% of $100 = $2`
    
5.  `Person B’s Commission: 3% of $100 = $3`
    
6.  `Person C’s Commission: 25% of $100 = $25`
    

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/referrals#important-notes)

Important Notes

*   Commissions Are Based on Bloom Bot’s 1% Fee.
    
*   All revenue share percentages are calculated from the standard 1% fee, regardless of any discounts applied to the user.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/referrals#id-10-referred-cashback)

**10% Referred Cashback**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you join Bloom through a referral link, you’ll automatically unlock a 10% cashback on our standard trading fees. Every trade you make generates cashback based on your trading volume, and your rewards are visible at all times inside the Referral Menu.

**How to get your 10% Cashback**[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/referrals#how-to-get-your-10-cashback)

1.  Sign up through a referral link.
    
2.  Start trading and automatically benefit from a 10% cashback on your trading volume.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/referrals#payouts)

Payouts


----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Cashback and referral fees are available for claim every 6 hours. To process a claim, your unclaimed balance must exceed the tresholds.

If your balance is below this threshold, you’ll simply need to wait until it accumulates above the minimum before claiming.

Blockchain

Minimum Amount Needed

SOL

0.1 SOL

ETH

0.01 ETH

BASE

0.01 ETH

BSC

0.05 BNB

HYPEREVM

1 HYPE

PLASMA

50 XPL

MONAD

1000 MON

To start using Bloom, please click the `Continue` button on Telegram.

By clicking `Continue`, you confirm that you have read, understood, and agree to our [Terms and Conditions](https://tos.bloombot.app/)
 and [Privacy Policy](https://tos.bloombot.app/)
.

If you do not agree to these terms, access to Bloom won't be possible, as the bot won't open.

# Live Stream PNL | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good night

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

The Live-Stream PnL Tracker lets you showcase your performance to viewers effortlessly. Easily integrated with OBS, it can be reset anytime as needed. The tracker automatically detects your wallet balance, ensuring real-time updates.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3158159183-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAZVSZEL47N9f4qOtz3Wz%252Fuploads%252FqEdNwCxdLiytfjmhrAnu%252Fstreamer.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf341981-66e2-4918-ae6e-17d671c5d85e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=323521ab&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/live-stream-pnl#installation-guide)

Installation Guide


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/live-stream-pnl#choose-your-pnl-sol-bsc)

Choose Your PNL (SOL / BSC)

SOL[](https://docs.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/live-stream-pnl#sol)

#### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/live-stream-pnl#single-wallet)

Single Wallet

[https://www.bloombot.app/streamer-pnl?chain=`sol`&wallet=`YOUR_ADDRESS`&ref\_code=`YOUR_REF_CODE`&bg=`DESIRED_BACKGROUND`](https://www.bloombot.app/streamer-pnl?chain=sol&wallet=YOUR_ADDRESS&ref_code=YOUR_REF_CODE&bg=DESIRED_BACKGROUND)

#### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/live-stream-pnl#multi-wallet)

Multi-Wallet

[https://www.bloombot.app/streamer-pnl?chain=sol&wallet1=`YOUR_ADDRESS`,wallet2=`YOUR_ADDRESS`,wallet3=`YOUR_ADDRESS`&ref\_code=`YOUR_REF_CODE`&bg=`DESIRED_BACKGROUND`](https://www.bloombot.app/streamer-pnl?chain=sol&wallet1=YOUR_ADDRESS,wallet2=YOUR_ADDRESS,wallet3=YOUR_ADDRESS&ref_code=YOUR_REF_CODE&bg=DESIRED_BACKGROUND)

BSC[](https://docs.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/live-stream-pnl#bsc)

[https://www.bloombot.app/streamer-pnl?chain=`bsc`&wallet=`YOUR_ADDRESS`&ref\_code=`YOUR_REF_CODE`&bg=`DESIRED_BACKGROUND`](https://ombot.app/streamer-pnl?chain=bsc&wallet=YOUR_ADDRESS&ref_code=YOUR_REF_CODE&bg=DESIRED_BACKGROUND)

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/live-stream-pnl#set-up)

Set up


------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Open your chosen link from the two options displayed above.
    
2.  Replace the parameters:
    
    1.  `YOUR_ADDRESS` – with your SOL or BSC wallet address.
        
    2.  `YOUR_REF_CODE` – with your referral code (e.g. Bloom).
        
    3.  `DESIRED_BACKGROUND` – with your chosen background design from the options below. If you don’t select a background, one will be chosen randomly.
        
    
3.  Copy the full URL
    

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/live-stream-pnl#add-to-obs)

Add to OBS


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Open OBS.
    
2.  Go to `Sources`.
    
3.  Click `+` → Select `Browser`.
    
4.  Paste your full custom URL.
    
5.  Set the recommended dimensions:
    
    1.  Width – `384`
        
    2.  Height – `147`
        
    

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/live-stream-pnl#starting-pnl-edit)

Starting PNL edit


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  In OBS Sources list.
    
2.  Right-click the browser source.
    
3.  Select `Interact`.
    
4.  Use `CTRL+B` (Windows) or `CMD+B` (Mac).
    
5.  Adjust PNL settings as needed.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/live-stream-pnl#link-examples)

Link Examples


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

SOL:

BSC:

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/live-stream-pnl#backgrounds)

Backgrounds


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Fees Structure | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good night

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

#### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/fees-structure#at-bloom-transparency-is-at-the-heart-of-everything-we-do)

**At Bloom, transparency is at the heart of everything we do.**

To keep our platform running smoothly and to continue providing the best possible trading experience, we charge a `1% fee` on every buy and sell transaction.

By signing in through a **referral**, you can benefit from a **reduced fee of 0.9%** `(10% discount)` instead of the standard 1% on all your transactions.

This small fee allows us to constantly improve the platform, add new features, and support the incredible Bloom community as it grows.

Why Fees?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/fees-structure#why-fees)

*   **Developers**: Ensuring continuous platform improvements and new feature development.
    
*   **Infrastructure**: Maintaining servers and systems to provide a smooth trading experience.
    
*   **Testing**: Ongoing testing to ensure stability, security, and optimal performance.
    
*   **Marketing**: Expanding Bloom’s reach and attracting new users to grow the community.
    
*   **Team**: Supporting the dedicated team that drives Bloom’s development and operations.
    

[PreviousReferrals](https://docs.bloombot.app/grow-with-bloom/referrals)
[NextLive Stream PNL](https://docs.bloombot.app/miscellaneous/live-stream-pnl)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Welcome | Extension | Bloom

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3058400886-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fz2QdoaScujkQBx5Lf47O%252Fuploads%252FXkOsnuJjyajM4I5tncOk%252FTwitter_header_-_7_0-00-02-01.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70e4f496-ce2c-4b69-9bb7-a8925299649b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7363fcd3&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension#how-it-works)

How It Works

The Bloom Extension brings Telegram trading directly into your web terminal, combining speed, automation, and flexibility in a single workflow. You keep using your preferred terminal, enhanced with Bloom’s execution engine and tools.

The Bloom Extension enhances your existing terminal rather than replacing it, delivering faster fills, deeper customization, seamless mobile trading, and powerful automation through one unified experience.

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension#what-you-get)

What You Get

**Unified Trading**

*   Telegram trading power embedded inside your terminal
    
*   No need to switch between Telegram and terminal interfaces
    

**Faster Execution**

*   Significantly faster fills compared to terminals alone
    
*   One-click trades via the integrated Quick Panel
    

**Quick Panel**

*   Execute trades without leaving the terminal
    
*   Switch strategies instantly using presets
    
*   Trade with one or multiple wallets
    

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension#customization-and-control)

Customization & Control

**Presets**

*   Create and manage multiple trading presets
    
*   Configure settings via web and Telegram
    
*   Tailor setups for different order types and scenarios
    

**Wallet Management**

*   Import your terminal wallet into Telegram in a few clicks
    
*   Track trades and PnL from desktop or mobile
    
*   Web-based setup with minimal Telegram interaction
    

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension#desktop-and-mobile-seamlessly)

Desktop and Mobile, Seamlessly

**Hybrid Trading**

*   Desktop: terminal + Quick Panel
    
*   Mobile: Bloom Telegram bot
    
*   Same wallets, presets, and strategies across devices
    
*   No complex mobile terminal apps required
    

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension#automation)

Automation

**Advanced Tools**

*   Telegram and Discord auto-buy scrapers
    
*   Instant execution on new token announcements
    
*   Reduced reaction time and manual effort
    

[NextDownload](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/getting-started/download)

# Activation | Extension | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

##### Good night

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

AI Based on your context

Send

Extension activation works the same for both Solana and EVM.

The activation code is sent to the Solana bot for the Solana extension, or to the EVM bot for the EVM extension.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/getting-started/activation#activation-steps)

Activation Steps


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

Click Get Code.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3058400886-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fz2QdoaScujkQBx5Lf47O%252Fuploads%252FNJEweQDmMOTksMOu6UPk%252Fget%2520code.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6ad34567-66e6-4957-bc14-c6367e55c15a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=27895ba4&sv=2)

2

You’ll be redirected to Bloom on Telegram, where your activation code is sent. Never share this code.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3058400886-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fz2QdoaScujkQBx5Lf47O%252Fuploads%252FldMmAGm4sXOlEmhyPqvs%252Fcode%2520tg.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd435d64a-6e8c-46c2-8515-2a969f1cc758&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72af2774&sv=2)

3

Copy and paste the code into the extension.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3058400886-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fz2QdoaScujkQBx5Lf47O%252Fuploads%252FS1GKVJOSiyM74Be4UQTO%252Fcode.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8050821c-95c4-493f-8219-f34cc6fe2301&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d902e7f7&sv=2)

4

Click Verify.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3058400886-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fz2QdoaScujkQBx5Lf47O%252Fuploads%252FaZYmLI9V9Vd28VahNIBH%252Fverify.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0fb3f211-3272-4cf4-bac2-1a692768452d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=59fd53e8&sv=2)

5

The extension refreshes and activate.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3058400886-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fz2QdoaScujkQBx5Lf47O%252Fuploads%252F3qv1Rg0lbNzNBhkft5eJ%252Fext%2520active.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7f80a34-1047-436f-8300-8f11f8d4f3ce&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e790a0a&sv=2)

* * *

Button

Action

Quick Buy Amount

Set your preferred amount for the Quick Buy buttons ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3058400886-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fz2QdoaScujkQBx5Lf47O%252Fuploads%252Fp6De0lXf7uStT9eucZcr%252FScreenshot%25202025-12-19%2520alle%252011.07.42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4802088a-fd5b-4922-8102-860de88a754f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e2848b09&sv=2)

Region

Select the desired region (EU1, US1)

Settings

Tap to open the extension settings.

Logout

Tap to logout.

Reset

Tap to reset the Quick Panel size across all tabs.

[NextSettings](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/settings)

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/getting-started/download#important)

Important


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Always make sure you are using the official Bloom Extension. We are not responsible for any unofficial or fake versions.

We understand that browser extensions can raise concerns, especially for crypto users. The Bloom Extension has been reviewed and verified by Google and only adds Bloom Buy and Snipe buttons to supported trading terminals.

The extension will never ask for private keys, wallet access, or transaction signatures, and it does not store or collect any user data.

* * *

You can download the Bloom Extension either from the Chrome Web Store or as a .zip file directly from our [website](https://bloombot.app/extension)
 linked below.

[![Logo](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fframerusercontent.com%2Fimages%2FWoYA5ZNm1E6WGGtlUuv5vpWeJOI.png&width=20&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=78059e49&sv=2)Bloom | The most advanced cross-chain trading automationbloombot.app](https://bloombot.app/extension)

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3058400886-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fz2QdoaScujkQBx5Lf47O%252Fuploads%252F7OrsIdmDnlICQik2G0Qk%252FScreenshot%25202026-01-05%2520alle%252020.54.12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dadcbb7ca-7ae0-4a29-8f3e-6d30ef05a562&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bea6f167&sv=2)

# Split Tokens | Extension | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good night

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

The Split Tokens feature allows you to distribute (or split) tokens from a sender wallet to one or more receiver wallets in a single action.

The system automatically detects which token to split based on the token page where the panel is currently open.

**Example:**

If you have the panel open on the $TEST token page, the split operation will automatically apply to $TEST.

# Discord | Extension | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good night

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/scrapers/discord#auto-buy)

Auto Buy


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Auto Buy executes buy transactions when a contract address is posted in the selected Telegram or Discord channel.

Keep the target channel open so the extension can continuously monitor it and trigger buys.

If both SOL and EVM extensions are active, Bloom automatically detects the blockchain and applies the correct Quick Buy behavior.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/scrapers/discord#running-auto-buy)

Running Auto Buy


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

Keep only one Discord Web tab open per window. Multiple tabs in the same window will disable Auto Buy.

2

Leave the target Discord tab open while Auto Buy is enabled.

3

Set the Auto Buy Amount in Scraper Settings before enabling the feature.

4

Tap Start EVM Auto Buy on Discord to begin.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3058400886-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fz2QdoaScujkQBx5Lf47O%252Fuploads%252FnLwwV4vASThOFaUXPlIK%252FSOL.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0abac078-8948-4709-8375-717274728de7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1cb4ce34&sv=2)

How to run multiple tabs?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/scrapers/discord#how-to-run-multiple-tabs)

To run multiple Telegram tabs, open one tab per separate PC window.

[PreviousScrapers](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/scrapers)
[NextTelegram](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/scrapers/telegram)

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/scrapers/telegram#auto-buy)

Auto Buy


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Auto Buy executes buy transactions when a contract address is posted in the selected Telegram or Discord channel.

Keep the target channel open so the extension can continuously monitor it and trigger buys.

If both SOL and EVM extensions are active, Bloom automatically detects the blockchain and applies the correct Quick Buy behavior.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/scrapers/telegram#running-auto-buy)

Running Auto Buy


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

Use **Telegram K** to enable Bloom’s Telegram Web feature. You can switch versions from Telegram Settings, as shown below.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3058400886-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fz2QdoaScujkQBx5Lf47O%252Fuploads%252FC75l9D5dRZGy82Ybmlzg%252Fk.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D180fe73d-be49-4de9-bc4e-96d415c6eb9a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72aff5aa&sv=2)

2

Keep only one Telegram Web tab open per window. Multiple tabs in the same window will disable Auto Buy.

3

Leave the target Telegram tab open while Auto Buy is enabled.

4

Set the Auto Buy Amount in Scraper Settings before enabling the feature.

5

Tap Start EVM Auto Buy on Telegram to begin.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3058400886-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fz2QdoaScujkQBx5Lf47O%252Fuploads%252FSRqOvm7KmQd2UiC6Qsi2%252FSOL.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a0d3d28-fe91-4937-bc8e-1cbb6a340b47&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fa6a47b3&sv=2)

How to run multiple tabs?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/scrapers/telegram#how-to-run-multiple-tabs)

To run multiple Telegram tabs, open one tab per separate PC window.

# Presets | Extension | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good night

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

The Preset Manager allows you to customize your Quick Panel presets. You can create multiple presets tailored to your trading needs, and they will be available across all supported platforms.

* * *

Field

Action

Preset Label

Enter the name you’d like to assign to the preset.

Buy Amounts

Enter the buy amounts you want to display.

Sell Percentages

Enter the percentages you want to sell.

Buy Fee

Set the transaction fee for buying.

Buy Tip

Set the Jito buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Buy Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

Sell Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

Sell Tip

Set the Jito sell tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Sell Slippage

Set the sell slippage percentage.

Anti-MEV for Buys

The fastest processor is automatically used to ensure maximum transaction success while buying, whether MEV Protection is enabled or disabled.

Anti-MEV for Sells

The fastest processor is automatically used to ensure maximum transaction success while selling, whether MEV Protection is Oenabled or disabled.

Auto Tip

If enabled, it automatically selects the Jito-suggested tip.

_Priority fees are set to a fixed amount since the tip is what matters for Jito Blocks._

Save Preset

Tap to save the current preset.

Load Defaults

Tap to load the default settings for customization.

[PreviousSettings](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/settings)
[NextScrapers](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/settings/scrapers)

Last updated 6 days ago

# Scrapers | Extension | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good night

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

Scraper Settings let you customize Discord and Telegram Auto Buy features.

Open the specific Telegram or Discord channel you want to monitor and keep it open. The extension continuously scans the channel and automatically triggers a buy when a contract address is posted.

* * *

Field

Action

Discord Auto Buy Amount

Set the amount you want to buy when Discord Auto Buy is enabled. This amount will apply to all contract addresses posted in the target channel.

Telegram Auto Buy Amount

Set the amount you want to buy when Telegram Auto Buy is enabled. This amount will apply to all contract addresses posted in the target channel.

Auto Buy Processor Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Auto Buy Priority Fee

Set the transaction fee for buying.

Min Volume

Set the minimum token volume you are willing to buy at.

Max Volume

Set the maximum token volume you are willing to buy at.

Min Market Cap

Set the minimum market cap you are willing to buy at.

Max Market Cap

Set the maximum market cap you are willing to buy at.

Skip contract if previously bought

If enabled, it will skip a contract address if it has already been posted in the current target channel where Auto Buy is active.

[PreviousPresets](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/settings/presets)
[NextLimit Orders](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/settings/limit-orders)

# Wallets | Extension | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good night

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

Bloom’s Wallet Settings let you choose how your purchase amounts are handled across active wallets. You can either buy the full amount in each wallet or split the total evenly across multiple wallets.

**Split Amount:** The buy amount is divided equally across all active wallets. Example: 1 SOL with 5 wallets = 0.2 SOL per wallet.

**Full Amount Each:** Each active wallet buys the full specified amount. Example: 1 SOL with 5 wallets = 1 SOL per wallet (5 SOL total).

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/settings/wallets#active-wallets)

Active Wallets

Select the wallets you’d like to activate by default for multi-wallet trades. You can easily change this selection later from the Quick Panel.

If you’ve added or removed a wallet, or if your wallets aren’t showing up correctly, click ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3058400886-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fz2QdoaScujkQBx5Lf47O%252Fuploads%252F2EKl42G2hv2clFd81aU1%252FScreenshot%25202025-12-19%2520alle%252011.36.32.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D653e21c6-749f-49dc-b723-9b388cda0441&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c49305c3&sv=2) to refresh the wallets.

[PreviousSites](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/settings/sites)
[NextAppearance](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/settings/appearance)

# Limit Orders | Extension | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good night

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

Limit Orders in the extension work on top of each platform’s native order system.

To create a limit order, you must use the platform’s own order flow (for example Axiom orders), triggered through Bloom’s dedicated button.

*   Create and manage limit orders directly from the extension
    
*   All created orders are also visible on the Telegram bot
    
*   Access orders on Telegram via /orders or the dedicated menu
    

#### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/settings/limit-orders#supported-platforms)

Supported Platforms

Currently supported platforms are Axiom, Photon, and BullX.

#### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/settings/limit-orders#usage-limits)

Usage limits

*   Up to 1000 active orders at the same time
    
*   Up to 10 orders per configuration
    

* * *

Field

Action

Limit Buy Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

Limit Sell Slippage

Set the sell slippage percentage.

Limit Buy Priority Fee

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Limit Sell Priority Fee

Set the sell tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Limit Buy Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Limit Sell Tip

Set the sell tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Allow High Impact

Lets your transaction be processed faster, even if it may cause a higher impact on the buy price.

Anti-MEV for Limit Buys

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

Anti-MEV for Limit Sells

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/settings/limit-orders#dev-sell)

Dev Sell


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This section lets you configure Dev Sell settings.

Once enabled, the Dev Sell button appears directly in the Quick Panel, allowing fast access during trading.

To enable the Dev Sell fields, you must first select one or both checkboxes.

Field

Action

Automatically sell when dev sells

Choose whether to automatically sell the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. If enabled, the bot will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

Add Dev Sell button to Panel

Add the Dev Sell button to the Quick Panel.

Trigger When Dev Sells All

Choose whether to sell automatically only when the developer sells 100 % of their tokens.

Buy Amount

Set the amount to be bought in SOL.

Sell Amount

Set the percentage amount to be sold.

Buy Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

Sell Slippage

Set the sell slippage percentage.

Buy Priority Fee

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Sell Priority Fee

Set the sell tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Buy Bundle Tip

Set the Jito buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Sell Bundle Tip

Set the Jito sell tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

[PreviousScrapers](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/settings/scrapers)
[NextSites](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/sol/settings/sites)

Last updated 6 days ago

# Presets | Extension | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

The Preset Manager allows you to customize your Quick Panel presets. You can create multiple presets tailored to your trading needs, and they will be available across all supported platforms.

* * *

Field

Action

Configure Preset For Chain

Select the blockchain you want to create presets for: ETH, BSC, MONAD, HYPEREVM, BASE.

Preset Name

Enter the name you’d like to assign to the preset.

Buy Amounts

Enter the buy amounts you want to display.

Buy Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

Buy Fee

Set the transaction fee for buying.

Buy Bundle Tip

Set the target buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Sell Amounts

Enter the percentages you want to sell.

Sell Slippage

Set the sell slippage percentage.

Sell Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

Sell Bundle Tip

Set the target buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Anti-MEV for Buys

When MEV Protect is enabled, your transactions will be processed through BloXroute to prevent getting MEVed. If disabled, transactions will be routed through the custom node.

Anti-MEV for Sells

When MEV Protect is enabled, your transactions will be processed through BloXroute to prevent getting MEVed. If disabled, transactions will be routed through the custom node.

Save Preset

Tap to save the current preset.

Load Defaults

Tap to load the default settings for customization.

[PreviousSettings](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/evm/settings)
[NextScrapers](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/evm/settings/scrapers)

Auto Buy


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Auto Buy executes buy transactions when a contract address is posted in the selected Telegram or Discord channel.

Keep the target channel open so the extension can continuously monitor it and trigger buys.

If both SOL and EVM extensions are active, Bloom automatically detects the blockchain and applies the correct Quick Buy behavior.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/extension/evm/scrapers/discord#running-auto-buy)

Running Auto Buy


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

Keep only one Discord Web tab open per window. Multiple tabs in the same window will disable Auto Buy.

2

Leave the target Discord tab open while Auto Buy is enabled.

3

Set the Auto Buy Amount in Scraper Settings before enabling the feature.

4

Tap Start EVM Auto Buy on Discord to begin.

Send

Scraper Settings let you customize Discord and Telegram Auto Buy features.

Open the specific Telegram or Discord channel you want to monitor and keep it open. The extension continuously scans the channel and automatically triggers a buy when a contract address is posted.

* * *

Field

Action

Configure Scraper For Chain

Select the blockchain you want to create presets for: ETH, BSC, BASE, or HYPEREVM.

Buy Amount

Set the amount you want to buy when the scraper is turned on. This amount will apply to all contract addresses posted in the target channel.

Buy Fee

Set the transaction gas (Max Priority Fee) for buying.

Buy Bundle Tip

Set the target buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Buy Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

Min Liquidity

Set the minimum pool liquidity required for a buy to execute.

Max Liquidity

Set the maximum pool liquidity required for a buy to execute.

Min Market Cap

Set the minimum market cap you are willing to buy at.

Max Market Cap

Set the maximum market cap you are willing to buy at.

Skip contract if previously bought

If enabled, it will skip a contract address if it has already been posted in the current target channel where Auto Buy is active.

Save Preset

Tap to save the current preset.

Load Defaults

Tap to load the default settings for customization.

# Pro Accounts | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good evening

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

**PRO Accounts are mandatory**. If the selected wallet doesn’t have one, Bloom will automatically attempt to create it. You’ll only see a confirmation, or a failure notification, once the creation transaction is processed.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#introduction-to-pro-accounts-v2.0)

Introduction to Pro Accounts (v2.0)


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Pro Accounts in version 2.0 are designed to optimize the broadcasting of your transactions across the best validators and node providers. This ensures that each buy or sell transaction you execute is handled efficiently and lands only once, avoiding duplication.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#usage-recommendations)

Usage Recommendations


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For typical activities such as running several copy tasks, placing orders, and performing spot trades—we generally recommend:

*   **1 to 3 Spot Pro Accounts**
    
*   **4 Task Pro Accounts**
    

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#types-of-pro-accounts)

Types of Pro Accounts


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Spot Accounts**[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#spot-accounts)

Used for any spot buy and sell operations, including those executed through our extension.

**Tasks Accounts**[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#tasks-accounts)

Used for copy-trading, AFK mode, and various types of orders.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#determining-the-number-of-pro-accounts-needed)

Determining the Number of Pro Accounts Needed


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The required number of Pro Accounts primarily depends on how many tasks you trigger at the same time. For instance, if you have only one Pro Account and two copy tasks that need to execute transactions simultaneously, only one transaction will successfully land.

In short, the more tasks you plan to run simultaneously, the more Pro Accounts you'll need to create.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#cost)

Cost


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each Pro Account requires a maximum of **0.002 SOL** for its creation.

[PreviousWallets](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets)
[NextBuy](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/buy)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [Introduction to Pro Accounts (v2.0)](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#introduction-to-pro-accounts-v2.0)
    
*   [Usage Recommendations](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#usage-recommendations)
    
*   [Types of Pro Accounts](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#types-of-pro-accounts)
    
*   [Determining the Number of Pro Accounts Needed](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#determining-the-number-of-pro-accounts-needed)
    
*   [Cost](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets/pro-accounts#cost)

# Limit Orders | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good afternoon

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

Limit orders allow you to set a specific price at which you want to buy or sell a cryptocurrency. Unlike market orders that execute immediately at the current price, limit orders only trigger when the market reaches your desired price or market cap.

Additionally, you can customize your order with multiple parameters, ensuring your trade is tailored to your strategy.

**Usage Limits:**

You can have a maximum of 1,000 active orders at any time, with a limit of 10 active orders per configuration

[PreviousSell](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/sell)
[NextLimit Buy](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/limit-orders/limit-buy)

# PnL Calendar | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good afternoon

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

The PnL Calendar is the easiest way to keep track of your trading performance inside Bloom.

It gives you a day-by-day view of your results for each month, helps you analyze your performance, and allows you to instantly generate a recap image that can be shared on Twitter \[X\] in one tap.

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/pnl-calendar#how-to-use-the-pnl-calendar)

How to Use the PnL Calendar


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Select the month**
    
    Pick the month you want to generate the PnL data for.
    
*   **Select the week**
    
    Narrow down your view by choosing a specific week within that month.
    
*   **Choose the format**
    
    Decide if you’d like to see your PnL results in the blockchain’s native currency or converted into USD.
    
*   **Generate your recap**
    
    Tap Generate Recap to create a visual monthly PnL recap image.
    
*   **Share your performance**
    
    Tap Share to instantly post your PnL recap on Twitter \[X\].
    

[PreviousSuggestions](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/suggestions)
[NextFAQs](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Withdraw | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good afternoon

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

**Always keep your address locked when not making updates. It’s one of the most effective measures to protect your funds from unauthorized access or malicious attacks.**

* * *

*   Access `💸 Withdraw` easily from the home menu or by using the `/withdraw` command.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FoyeWAKuRNaLUIHMLIgaV%252FWithd.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7ec9c2b-e9bf-49cc-8ea9-801cddfb5504&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1ad75ab1&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F4kSVWmF4zzbP17j6B0sP%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb12963b-e466-47aa-ab0e-6c329cbb3059&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cc549511&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

50%, 100%

Preset percentage of SOL you want to withdraw (e.g., 50% withdraws half your funds).

X SOL

Edit the amount of SOL you wish to withdraw.

Set Address

Set the address to receive your funds.

Please enter your Solana withdrawal address:

Lock Address

Lock your address to prevent changes. This safety measure ensures that no malicious party can modify the address or withdraw your funds for 24 hours unlocking it.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FCtrv66BadLitK5Um2yYf%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252016.27.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f6d77d2-d63a-4974-98f1-14d5c9223d97&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fb404e3e&sv=2)

Unlock Address

Unlock your address if you need to make changes. A 24-hour security cooldown will be applied before any modifications are allowed.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F7lbgQtUAmgbWAke2uk7Q%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252016.27.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3700a0b-bb19-4746-8c87-4b3d734f8d6a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=55616398&sv=2)

Back

Return to the previous page.

Refresh

Refresh the menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/withdraw#locking-unlocking-withdraw-address)

Locking/Unlocking Withdraw Address


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Protecting your funds is our top priority, and we’ve implemented a safety feature to help safeguard your wallet: Address Locking.

🔒 Why locking your address?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/withdraw#why-locking-your-address)

Locking your address ensures it cannot be changed while locked, making it impossible for anyone—including potential attackers—to replace it and withdraw your funds. This is a critical layer of security, especially in case of a malicious attack or if your wallet becomes compromised.

🔓 Unlocking your address[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/withdraw#unlocking-your-address)

If you need to make changes to your address, you must first unlock it. Once unlocked, a 24-hour security cooldown begins, ensuring that no changes can be made during this time. This delay provides a buffer to detect and prevent unauthorized attempts.

[PreviousPositions](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/positions)
[NextReferrals](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/referrals)

# Quick Query Ticker | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good afternoon

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

The Quick Query Ticker feature lets you instantly retrieve essential token information directly through our Telegram bot. Simply input the token ticker using the `$` symbol followed by the ticker name (e.g., `$TRUMP`).

#### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/telegram-commands/quick-query-ticker#how-it-works)

How It Works:

1.  Open the Bloom Telegram bot.
    
2.  Type the ticker preceded by `$` (e.g., `$TICKER`).
    
3.  Hit send to instantly view the data.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FM8wiPpFDlJwlCHZBUStw%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-19%2520alle%252001.38.07.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd4a0e4d-e066-4728-bbbe-a0af28aaaa6b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a558ab72&sv=2)

# Copy Limit Orders | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good afternoon

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

**Usage Limits:**

You can have a maximum of 1,000 active orders at any time, with a limit of 10 active orders per configuration

*   Access `🤖 Copy Trade` easily from the home menu or by using the `/afk` command.
    
*   Click `🆕 Add New Config` or an already existing config.
    
*   Click `📈 Limit Orders`.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fpbi7IXYpA3u0jPckFhMz%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252017.32.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8716f39-a533-43f2-ba7d-439eec3becc2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c0a17d3&sv=2)

*   Click `🆕 Create Limit Order`.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FIOnv8S50bInsqZrZbcI9%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252017.33.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a877771-6084-4509-9218-b2aecdbcd453&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=44f29b70&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FMJtMy8W7TNG55MSKCD5G%252FAuto%2520orders.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7aebd1d-0ac1-4765-acfa-9aec7801287d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9dcc8264&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Dev Sell

Choose whether to automatically sell the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. 🟢: When enabled, Bloom will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Time

Sell after a desired timespan. **Enter the expiry time in:**

• 1H = 1 hour

• 30M = 30 minutes

• 1D = 1 day

• 60 = 60 seconds

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Trailing

A Trailing Stop Loss moves automatically as the token price increases. The Trailing Value (%) represents the distance between the current price and where the stop loss is set. As the token price rises, the stop loss moves up with it, always maintaining that distance. If the price drops enough to hit the trailing level, the order triggers and closes the position automatically.

Profit/Loss %

Set take profit or stop loss. • 📈 **Take Profit:** Use positive values (e.g., +100% for 2x)

• 📉 **Stop Loss:** Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)

Fixed Mcap

Set the target market cap at which you’d like Bloom to sell.

Mcap Variation

Set the market cap increase or decrease threshold at which you’d like Bloom to sell. Bloom will execute the sale only when the market cap change matches your specified value.

Sell at

This button adapts based on your selected selling method (Profit/Loss %, Fixed MCap, MCap Variation), allowing you to set your preferred value accordingly.

Enter your target value:

• Take Profit: e.g. 50%, 150%.

• Stop Loss: e.g. -20%, -50%.

Examples:

• Profit %: 100%: your holdings will be sold at 2x.

• Loss %: -50%: your holdings will be sold when the price drops by 50%.

Notes:

• Only one % value (TP or SL) per limit order.

Sell Amount

Set the target amount to sell as a percentage.

Please enter your desired sell amount:

Example:

• For a sell of 10%, enter 10

Slippage

Set the slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Sell Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

High Impact (Expert only)

Enables trades that require higher price impact than usual. Use this if you’re buying large amounts of SOL in low-liquidity pools. ⚠️ **Expert users only:** using this when it’s not needed can route the sale through suboptimal pools or cause bad slippage.

Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

Please enter your desired priority fee:

Example:

• For a priority fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Back

Return to the previous menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

Once the orders are created, you can edit them by selecting the target order or cancel them by clicking `🗑️ Delete Order` in the dedicated menu, as shown below.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F90Ic9itInCwdLGrgDU82%252FAuto%2520orders.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4101ba1-5963-493c-8f02-7f3623defbba&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=20a4d489&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Dev Sell

Choose whether to automatically sell the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. 🟢: When enabled, Bloom will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Time

Sell after a desired timespan. **Enter the expiry time in:**

• 1H = 1 hour

• 30M = 30 minutes

• 1D = 1 day

• 60 = 60 seconds

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Trailing

A Trailing Stop Loss moves automatically as the token price increases. The Trailing Value (%) represents the distance between the current price and where the stop loss is set. As the token price rises, the stop loss moves up with it, always maintaining that distance. If the price drops enough to hit the trailing level, the order triggers and closes the position automatically.

Profit/Loss %

Set take profit or stop loss. • 📈 **Take Profit:** Use positive values (e.g., +100% for 2x)

• 📉 **Stop Loss:** Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)

Fixed Mcap

Set the target market cap at which you’d like Bloom to sell.

Mcap Variation

Set the market cap increase or decrease threshold at which you’d like Bloom to sell. Bloom will execute the sale only when the market cap change matches your specified value.

Sell at

This button adapts based on your selected selling method (Profit/Loss %, Fixed MCap, MCap Variation), allowing you to set your preferred value accordingly.

Enter your target value:

• Take Profit: e.g. 50%, 150%.

• Stop Loss: e.g. -20%, -50%.

Examples:

• Profit %: 100%: your holdings will be sold at 2x.

• Loss %: -50%: your holdings will be sold when the price drops by 50%.

Notes:

• Only one % value (TP or SL) per limit order.

Sell Amount

Set the target amount to sell as a percentage.

Please enter your desired sell amount:

Example:

• For a sell of 10%, enter 10

Slippage

Set the slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Sell Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

High Impact (Expert only)

Enables trades that require higher price impact than usual. Use this if you’re buying large amounts of SOL in low-liquidity pools. ⚠️ **Expert users only:** using this when it’s not needed can route the sale through suboptimal pools or cause bad slippage.

Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

Please enter your desired priority fee:

Example:

• For a priority fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Back

Return to the previous menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

Once the orders are created, you can edit them by selecting the target order or cancel them by clicking `🗑️ Delete Order` in the dedicated menu, as shown below.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fc3BThte0PlgtZal4UqJj%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252019.04.42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1df5a62-a21c-414b-bb1f-d4800b8b224b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cedd2a59&sv=2)

# Bridge | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good afternoon

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/bridge#what-bridging-means)

What bridging means?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bridging lets you move tokens from one blockchain (like Solana) to another (like Ethereum or Base) by locking or burning them on the original chain, then minting or unlocking an equivalent amount on the target chain. This process relies on cross-chain communication protocols or specialized smart contracts to verify that tokens were locked on the source chain before creating the new tokens on the destination. As a result, you maintain the same overall value while gaining access to DeFi opportunities that are unique to each blockchain.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/bridge#debridgepoints)

deBridgePoints

When you bridge through Bloom, you’ll earn deBridge points just as if you were bridging directly via deBridge itself.

* * *

*   Access `✈️ Bridge` easily from the home menu or by using the `/bridge` command.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FaGhMk0L8FdCwIRPu5btO%252Fsol.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfdb0b133-451f-4d32-8590-118f867701c1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ee570cf0&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F5UgAzANOwwYnoiAHRh1V%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-30%2520alle%252017.09.27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D071e23f3-acd5-4c26-bbd2-68512bd64de5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81388e8b&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/bridge#how-to-bridge)

How To Bridge


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From the SOL blockchain, you can directly bridge to BSC, Ethereum, and Base using Bloom.

*   SOL → BSC: Send SOL and receive BNB on BSC.
    
*   SOL → ETH: Send SOL and receive ETH on Ethereum.
    
*   SOL → BASE: Send SOL and receive ETH on Base.
    
*   SOL → HYPER EVM: Send SOL and receive HYPE on HYPER EVM.
    

*   Select the target receiver blockchain (BSC, ETH, BASE or HYPER EVM). Only one option can be active at a time.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FsPPZeBF171H0gaww58yt%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-30%2520alle%252017.09.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1fc73e27-c7ac-4301-b361-08eb4ff8be77&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6e8240de&sv=2)

*   You can set the receiving addresses needed—(BSC, ETH, BASE, HYPER EVM)—depending on your needs. Tap `💸 Set Address`, then enter your receiver address for the blockchain you’ve selected.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FETtKkCjwstkY9vpDtQfX%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252013.48.14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D636e0733-b65a-4dd9-a905-fb7f86747e16&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=883c1bb6&sv=2)

*   Double-check that all details match, then tap `✈️ Bridge` to transfer your funds.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FNffEtgyfwvsTg9WOwdkB%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-10%2520alle%252015.52.46.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1cba66c3-2259-43d7-bc36-87752ac6baf1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=91dda2a2&sv=2)

After bridging, if you’d like to switch the target receiving blockchain, ensure you select the new blockchain and eventually update the receiving wallet accordingly.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/bridge#locking-unlocking-withdraw-address)

Locking/Unlocking Withdraw Address


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Protecting your funds is our top priority, and we’ve implemented a safety feature to help safeguard your wallet: Address Locking.

Each address can be locked or unlocked independently.

Why locking your receiver address?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/bridge#why-locking-your-receiver-address)

Locking your receiver address ensures it cannot be changed while locked, making it impossible for anyone—including potential attackers—to replace it and bridge your funds. This is a critical layer of security, especially in case of a malicious attack or if your wallet becomes compromised.

Unlocking your receiver address[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/bridge#unlocking-your-receiver-address)

If you need to replace your receiver address, you must first unlock it. Once unlocked, a 24-hour security cooldown begins, ensuring that no changes can be made during this time. This delay provides a buffer to detect and prevent unauthorized attempts.

[PreviousReferrals](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/referrals)
[NextSuggestions](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/suggestions)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [How To Bridge](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/bridge#how-to-bridge)
    
*   [Locking/Unlocking Withdraw Address](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/bridge#locking-unlocking-withdraw-address)

# FAQs | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good afternoon

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

Is Bloom Bot free to use?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#is-bloom-bot-free-to-use)

Yes, Bloom Bot is completely free to use. We only charge a 1% fee on buy and sell transactions.

What is slippage?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-slippage)

Slippage is the difference between the expected price of a trade and the actual price at which the trade is executed. It typically occurs during periods of high volatility or low liquidity. Generally, the higher it is, the faster your transaction is but the higher are the chances of getting your transaction sandwiched.

What is market cap?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-market-cap)

Market cap is the total value of a cryptocurrency, calculated by multiplying price by circulating supply.

What is a buy and sell fee?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-a-buy-and-sell-fee)

The fee you are willing to pay to get your transaction processed.

Buy & Sell Protection ON/OFF[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#buy-and-sell-protection-on-off)

🟩 **Buy/Sell Protection ON:**

Only MEV-protected processors are used, significantly reducing sandwich attack risk (though a minimal chance remains).

🟥 **Buy/Sell Protection OFF:**

Transactions are broadcasted to all supported processors, including those without MEV protection.

What is a bundle fee?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-a-bundle-fee)

A bundle tip fee is an extra payment made to JITO's network of block producers to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

When is the contract renounced?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#when-is-the-contract-renounced)

A contract is renounced when the developer gives up control, making it immutable and decentralized.

What is freeze authority?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-freeze-authority)

Freeze authority allows a contract owner to pause or restrict transfers of tokens, usually for security reasons.

What is liquidity?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-liquidity)

Liquidity in cryptocurrency markets refers to the total amount of funds available in the liquidity pool.

What is a liquidity pool?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-a-liquidity-pool)

A liquidity pool is a smart contract where tokens are locked for the purpose of providing liquidity.

How do Auto Orders work?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#how-do-auto-orders-work)

Auto orders are limit orders automatically created after you buy a coin. They trigger based on your settings and don’t require you to start them manually once created.

What does Degen Mode do?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#what-does-degen-mode-do)

Degen Mode instantly buys a token as soon as its contract address is entered in Telegram, without asking for additional details. Once typed, it will attempt to purchase based on your settings, regardless of your balance.

What are Limit Orders?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#what-are-limit-orders)

Limit Orders let you define a specific price at which you want to buy or sell a cryptocurrency. Unlike market orders that execute immediately at the current price, limit orders only trigger when the market reaches your desired price or market cap.

Bloom goes a step further by allowing you to combine multiple parameters—enabling you to fully customize each limit order to match your personal strategy.

What is a deployer?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#what-is-a-deployer)

A deployer is the wallet address that initially creates and launches a cryptocurrency contract on the blockchain.

The deployer field is an optional filter you can use to better manage your sniper tasks. Here, you can enter the deployer wallet address to make sure you’re sniping the correct token. You can skip this filter if you’ve already selected the right platform from the Platforms menu.

[PreviousPnL Calendar](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/pnl-calendar)
[NextSupported DEXes/Tokens](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/supported-dexes-tokens)

Last updated 5 days ago

Send

Sniper orders must be created upfront directly from `Settings->Presets->Sniper Presets`.

Auto orders are limit orders automatically created after you buy a coin. They trigger based on your settings and don’t require you to start them manually once created.

After creation, the task will automatically start post-buy. Make sure to delete it if you don't want it to run.

**Usage Limits:**

You can have a maximum of 1,000 active orders at any time, with a limit of 10 active orders per configuration

* * *

Click `📈 Spot Presets`.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fpbi7IXYpA3u0jPckFhMz%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252017.32.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8716f39-a533-43f2-ba7d-439eec3becc2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c0a17d3&sv=2)

*   Click `🆕 Create Limit Order`.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FIOnv8S50bInsqZrZbcI9%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252017.33.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a877771-6084-4509-9218-b2aecdbcd453&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=44f29b70&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F1xqeNiWqPC1mOEn3MiG8%252FAuto%2520orders.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5ddc061-7ad0-461b-ad46-d7b002d642b2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=31e8e3ff&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Dev Sell

Choose whether to automatically sell the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. 🟢: When enabled, Bloom will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Time

Sell after a desired timespan. **Enter the expiry time in:**

• 1H = 1 hour

• 30M = 30 minutes

• 1D = 1 day

• 60 = 60 seconds

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Trailing

A Trailing Stop Loss moves automatically as the token price increases. The Trailing Value (%) represents the distance between the current price and where the stop loss is set. As the token price rises, the stop loss moves up with it, always maintaining that distance. If the price drops enough to hit the trailing level, the order triggers and closes the position automatically.

Profit/Loss %

Set take profit or stop loss. • 📈 **Take Profit:** Use positive values (e.g., +100% for 2x)

• 📉 **Stop Loss:** Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)

Fixed Mcap

Set the target market cap at which you’d like Bloom to sell.

Mcap Variation

Set the market cap increase or decrease threshold at which you’d like Bloom to sell. Bloom will execute the sale only when the market cap change matches your specified value.

Sell at

This button adapts based on your selected selling method (Profit/Loss %, Fixed MCap, MCap Variation), allowing you to set your preferred value accordingly.

Enter your target value:

• Take Profit: e.g. 50%, 150%.

• Stop Loss: e.g. -20%, -50%.

Examples:

• Profit %: 100%: your holdings will be sold at 2x.

• Loss %: -50%: your holdings will be sold when the price drops by 50%.

Notes:

• Only one % value (TP or SL) per limit order.

Sell Amount

Set the target amount to sell as a percentage.

Please enter your desired sell amount:

Example:

• For a sell of 10%, enter 10

Slippage

Set the slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Sell Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

High Impact (Expert only)

Enables trades that require higher price impact than usual. Use this if you’re buying large amounts of SOL in low-liquidity pools. ⚠️ **Expert users only:** using this when it’s not needed can route the sale through suboptimal pools or cause bad slippage.

Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

Please enter your desired priority fee:

Example:

• For a priority fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Back

Return to the previous menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

Once the orders are created, you can edit them by selecting the target order or cancel them by clicking `🗑️ Delete Order` in the dedicated menu, as shown below.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fc3BThte0PlgtZal4UqJj%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252019.04.42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1df5a62-a21c-414b-bb1f-d4800b8b224b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cedd2a59&sv=2)

Allows selling with higher price impact than usual. Useful for large sell orders in low-liquidity pools.

Choose whether to automatically buy the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. If enabled, the bot will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

Create Limit Order

Create the limit order.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/limit-orders/limit-sell#take-profit)

Take Profit


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set multiple Take Profits, create separate orders with different market caps/prices and percentages aligned with your goals and strategy.

To set a take-profit, enter a market cap or price higher than your entry price. If you prefer to use a percentage, create an [Auto Order](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/settings/presets/spot-presets-auto-orders)
 instead.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/limit-orders/limit-sell#stop-loss)

Stop Loss


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set multiple Stop Loss, create separate orders with different market caps/prices and percentages aligned with your goals and strategy.

To set a stop-loss, enter a market cap or price lower than your entry price. For percentage-based stops, use [Auto Orders](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/settings/presets/spot-presets-auto-orders)
.

# Degen Mode | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good afternoon

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

Degen Mode instantly buys a token as soon as its contract address is entered in Telegram, without asking for additional details. Once typed, it will attempt to purchase based on your settings, regardless of your balance.

*   When enabled, Degen Mode will attempt to **buy immediately as soon as the token address is entered**, even before the token menu appears. It will try to execute the purchase regardless of the wallet balance.
    
*   Once the token is sold, it won’t attempt to rebuy, even if auto-buy is enabled.
    

**🟢 ON –** Automatically buy a coin when the coin address is pasted. 🔴 **OFF –** Manually start buy when the coin address is pasted.

* * *

*   Access `⚙️ Settings` easily from the home menu or by using the `/settings`command.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FbgaXiaSbfRxMqYqMtwyQ%252FSettings.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd552293-8385-48b6-8ebd-88f2d507cf41&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=74c650a1&sv=2)

*   Tap `Degen Mode`.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FOgHSIlBWN01flKWPWx5y%252FDegen.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb762210-f491-4f40-8df8-ebfa424ef40c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cfdc917b&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fi4k4bdUtQuQwzNhObkGK%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252015.14.35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57b2cb79-df52-4cb8-bf1a-e18b7838d740&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6c1112da&sv=2)
