Send

Spot sell provides all the tools and settings you need to sell a coin with one or multiple wallets, set limit orders, take profit, stop loss and perform any sell action according to your preferences.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/sell#how-to-sell)

How to Sell


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enter the target token address (eg. `Z6TpfVZySS4vWcHrF22yzsa7nZRXQBKu2qjF9bNpump`) or click `↔️ Switch to Sell` from the buy menu.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FtidJ89wAJydEd7j6rKzh%252FScreenshot%25202025-07-09%2520alle%252014.07.33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e69f7ac-96f0-4a59-aad4-012120174f8e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=19b62c1e&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Switch to buy

[Refer to the dedicated guide.](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/buy)

Refresh

Refresh the menu.

Active Wallets

Choose the wallets you want to trade with.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FuwBflHPQwwzkfdSpXjXi%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252015.30.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D349c1b3d-18f1-4a93-b696-3fda77c51cd0&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8ef37dc0&sv=2)

10 % (example)

Choose the preset % to sell.

10 % (example)

Choose the preset % to sell.

10 % (example)

Choose the preset % to sell.

Initials

Submit a sell transaction to recover the cost, fee, and tip.

X %

Choose a custom % amount to sell.

Please enter your desired sell percentage:

• Choose the % to sell.

Example:

• If you want to sell 90% of your position, enter 90

X SOL

Choose a custom SOL amount to sell.

Please enter your desired sell amount in SOL:

Example:

• For a sell of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Sell Tip

**Only visible when Anti-MEV is disabled.** Set the sell tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Slippage

Set the slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Switch to Buy

Switch to Buy menu.

Limit Orders

[Set a sell limit order, take profit and stop loss.](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/limit-orders/limit-sell)

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fwc4mRHgL0fU7Y6OEdIPT%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-09%2520alle%252017.19.58.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D604f0dcd-7d1f-4e71-bbde-1ae0e7c3e679&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6ad3f228&sv=2)

Generate PnL

Generate the PnL pic.

PnL pic to be shared.

Auto Tip

If enabled, it automatically selects the Jito-suggested tip.

_Priority fees are set to a fixed amount since the tip is what matters for Jito Blocks._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Sell Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Split Tokens

Automatically split tokens from your wallet with the highest balance evenly across your selected wallets, completely emptying it.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F9JkMHMrwYZ1XGxHmQ4Il%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-05%2520alle%252017.58.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43d7a4e8-279f-49bf-8e8d-291d618efb47&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=627e15a9&sv=2)

Select the recipient wallet(s) and click `Split Tokens`.

View Chart

Opens the DexScreener Telegram mini-app, where you can view charts, transactions, bubblemaps, and other data.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FuFja6V51o16EvvsMRzsn%252FScreenshot%25202025-07-09%2520alle%252013.08.16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc63218a0-3e03-4985-ac09-7fc9458e4df1&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7fb20910&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/sell#multi-wallet-sell)

Multi-Wallet Sell


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To sell on multiple wallets, you need to select them first. Follow these steps:

*   Click `💰 Active Wallets`.
    
*   Activate or deactivate wallets based on your preferences.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FjM4uHCmk8RbqhRfnt1Zc%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252015.30.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3233dd19-d6d5-4a52-a688-adc38b31b5c0&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=51ae06fb&sv=2)

*   Once done, click `⬅️ Back` to return to the sell menu.

[NextLimit Orders](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/limit-orders)

Max Buy Count

Specify how many of the target account’s posted contracts you want the bot to purchase. e._g. • If you enter 1, Bloom will only buy the first contract posted. • If you enter 2, Bloom will buy both the first and the second contracts posted._

_If you change target account, the parameter won't reset._

Please enter your desired number of tokens to trade or enter -1 to disable:

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

🟢: When enabled, Bloom automatically buys contracts posted in a Twitter reply according to your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Min Market Cap

Set the minimum market cap at which you’re willing to buy. When the post appears, the bot checks the cap: if the market cap is below your threshold, the buy won’t execute; if it’s above that value, the buy will trigger.

Please enter your desired market cap or enter -1 to disable:

• Use K for thousands, M for millions, B for billions

Examples:

• $12 million: Enter 12M or 12000000

• $500,000: Enter 500K or 0.5M

Max Market Cap

Set the maximum market cap at which you’re willing to buy. The bot checks the cap when the post appears: if the market cap exceeds your threshold, the buy won’t trigger; if it’s lower, the buy will execute.

Please enter your desired market cap or enter -1 to disable:

• Use K for thousands, M for millions, B for billions

Examples:

• $12 million: Enter 12M or 12000000

• $500,000: Enter 500K or 0.5M

Min Token Age

• Set the minimum amount of time passed since the token was created. • For Pump.fun migrated coins, the time is calculated from the moment they bonded. _Note: Some older tokens may not work properly with this filter_

Please enter the token age or enter -1 to disable:

📝 Format examples:

• 1H = 1 hour

• 30M = 30 minutes

• 1D = 1 day

• 60 = 60 seconds

Supported units:

• H = hours

• M = minutes

• D = days

• Direct number = seconds

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F9JkMHMrwYZ1XGxHmQ4Il%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-05%2520alle%252017.58.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43d7a4e8-279f-49bf-8e8d-291d618efb47&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=627e15a9&sv=2)

Select the recipient wallet(s) and click `Split Tokens`.

View Chart

Opens the DexScreener Telegram mini-app, where you can view charts, transactions, bubblemaps, and other data.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fu7BB4gaqT1qYY0cC5Zcp%252FScreenshot%25202025-07-09%2520alle%252013.08.16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dce0b0b64-9cf4-4852-9d29-d677a2de12d5&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=474517c2&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/buy#multi-wallet-buy)

Multi-Wallet Buy


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To buy with multiple wallets, you need to select them first. Follow these steps:

*   Click `💰 Active Wallets`.
    
*   Activate or deactivate wallets based on your preferences.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FjM4uHCmk8RbqhRfnt1Zc%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252015.30.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3233dd19-d6d5-4a52-a688-adc38b31b5c0&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=51ae06fb&sv=2)

*   Once done, click `⬅️ Back` to return to the buy menu.

**Buy Fee –** The buy fee is taken from the default one in [settings](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/settings/fee)
.

**Orders expiration –** Expired orders are automatically deleted.

**Usage Limits:**

You can have a maximum of 1,000 active orders at any time, with a limit of 10 active orders per configuration

* * *

*   Start a regular [Buy](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/buy)
     task by entering the token address.
    
*   Tap `📈 Limit Orders`.

# Afk | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good afternoon

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

AFK Mode allows you to automate your trades while you’re away. By setting up key parameters and configurations, the bot will automatically execute buy and sell orders on your behalf based on your inputs.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/afk#benefits-of-afk-mode)

**Benefits of AFK Mode**

1.  **Trade effortlessly**: You can potentially make profits even while you’re away, as the bot manages trades for you.
    
2.  **Tailored settings**: You control how the bot operates with various parameters, ensuring it aligns with your trading strategy.
    
3.  **Multi-Testing:** With AFK Mode, you can run multiple trading setups simultaneously to find the most profitable and reliable strategy.
    

Setting up AFK Mode properly requires time and effort. A well-configured setup can maximize your chances of success, but it’s essential to carefully adjust the parameters to fit your goals.

* * *

*   Access `💤 AFK Mode` easily from the home menu or by using the `/afk` command.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F4J9zRS4SI0MVIJoWShA8%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df2dbb442-8c61-419f-af49-f2862b92c2e3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bdb15f3f&sv=2)

*   Tap `🆕 Add new config`.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F2KVOsFXAiFEQecqFOSn9%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-04%2520alle%252015.48.42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db584127d-c51b-4ce0-ace8-f140ac185a7c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c9a320dd&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Update the wallet currently in use, the change will apply to all active and inactive tasks.

Click the button to switch to another wallet.

Add new config

Add a new AFK configuration.

Pause All

Pause all active AFK configurations.

Start all the AFK configurations.

Choose the platform to activate the AFK task on. After selection, set up the task, and AFK Mode will be enabled on all chosen platforms.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fbxke5DCOTIOxRPJOX5o5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D49abbd8a-c31e-4c90-b60b-dc009e5d524e&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fa939200&sv=2)

Current Trades

Show how many times your configuration has bought that token.

Reset Count

Reset the number of times your configuration has bought that token.

Max Buy Count

Set the maximum number of coins the bot will purchase according to your current configuration.

Please enter your desired number of tokens to trade or enter -1 to disable:

Buy

Choose the SOL amount to buy.

Please enter your desired buy amount:

• Use SOL for direct amounts

Example:

• For a buy of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Fee

Set the transaction fee for buying.

Please enter your desired priority fee:

Example:

• For a priority fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Min Amount Out

Set the minimum number of tokens you want to receive.

Please enter your desired token value

• Use K for thousands, M for millions, B for billions

_Examples:_

• 12 million: Enter 12M or 12000000

• 500,000: Enter 500K or 0.5M

Buy Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Auto Tip

If enabled, it automatically selects the Jito-suggested tip.

_Priority fees are set to a fixed amount since the tip is what matters for Jito Blocks._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Tip

Set the target buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Min Creator Buy

Minimum amount of SOL the creator must buy of their own coin.

Set to 0 to allow the bot to buy coins even if the deployer hasn’t purchased any tokens.

Please enter your desired creator buy amount or enter -1 to disable

Max Creator Buy

Maximum amount of SOL the creator can buy of their own coin.

Set to 0 to allow the bot to buy coins regardless of the deployer’s purchase amount.

Please enter your desired creator buy amount or enter -1 to disable

Min Tokens Created

Minimum number of tokens created by the deployer on LaunchLab.

Please enter your desired tokens created or enter -1 to disable

Max Tokens Created

Maximum number of tokens created by the deployer on LaunchLab.

_If set to 1, and the deployer created a token in the past, it’s still valid if they create a new one and the bot buys it. The limit applies to tokens created after the bot starts monitoring._

Please enter your desired tokens created or enter -1 to disable

Min Tokens Migrated

Minimum number of tokens created by the deployer on LaunchLab that migrate to Raydium.

Please enter your desired min tokens migrated or enter -1 to disable

Safe Deployer

If enabled, it uses an external service to help identify and protect you from potential rugs. As this is a third-party service, we cannot guarantee 100% accuracy. While it may be slightly slower, it significantly improves your potential success rate.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Whitelisted Mint

Set whitelisted token address. Max 1 per field.

Please enter your desired mint address or enter -1 to disable:

Example:

• 9BB6NFEcjBCtnNLFko2FqVQBq8HHM13kCyYcdQbgpump

Whitelisted Deployer

Set whitelisted deployer. Max 1 per field.

Please enter your desired deployer address or enter -1 to disable:

Example:

• toAPhdPcxDZsm2ziAgKcLLb5FMvhsUxqWpRvxTnYfnP

Exact Name/Ticker

Set the whitelisted token name; it must exactly match the Name/Ticker _(eg. Pinko)_. • Max 1 per field. • _The field is_ _**not**_ _case sensitive._

Please enter your desired name or enter -1 to disable:

Example:

• BLOOM

Name/Ticker Contains

Set the whitelisted token name; it only needs to partially match the Name/Ticker _(eg. Pinko)_. • Max 1 per field. • _The field is_ _**not**_ _case sensitive._

Please enter your desired name contains or enter -1 to disable:

Example:

• SOL

LaunchCoin Handle

Enter the LaunchCoin handle.

Please enter your desired launch coin handle or enter -1 to disable:

_Examples:_

• BloomTrading or @BloomTrading

Start Time

Set your desired task starting time.

Enter the start time in 24h format:

Examples:

• 10:00:00 (10 AM UTC)

• 15:30:00 (3:30 PM UTC)

• 12 (12:00:00 PM UTC)

End Time

Set your desired task ending time.

Enter the end time in 24h format:

Examples:

• 10:00:00 (10 AM UTC)

• 15:30:00 (3:30 PM UTC)

• 12 (12:00:00 PM UTC)

Blacklist

Blacklist setup:

*   **Words:** set specific words contained in the token name to make the AFK task skip those tokens. You can also perform a **mass import** to add multiple words at once.
    
*   **Deployers:** add deployer addresses you want the AFK task to ignore when creating buy tasks. A **mass import** option is available here as well.
    

Limit Orders

[Refer to the dedicated guide.](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/afk/afk-limit-orders)

Active

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Duplicate config

Duplicate the current config.

Delete Config

Delete the current config.

Auto Orders


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Auto orders are limit orders automatically created after you buy a coin. They trigger based on your settings and don’t require you to start them manually once created.

After creation, the task will automatically start post-buy. Make sure to delete it if you don't want it to run.

*   Click `📈 Limit Orders`.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fpbi7IXYpA3u0jPckFhMz%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252017.32.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8716f39-a533-43f2-ba7d-439eec3becc2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c0a17d3&sv=2)

*   Click `🆕 Create Limit Order`.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FIOnv8S50bInsqZrZbcI9%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-27%2520alle%252017.33.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a877771-6084-4509-9218-b2aecdbcd453&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=44f29b70&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F6A1gdXc0Vm7r85WaN3kh%252FAuto%2520orders.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df489af85-cb64-4fd4-9216-1aab94d69b19&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3887afda&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Dev Sell

Choose whether to automatically sell the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. 🟢: When enabled, Bloom will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Time

Sell after a desired timespan. **Enter the expiry time in:**

• 1H = 1 hour

• 30M = 30 minutes

• 1D = 1 day

• 60 = 60 seconds

Trailing

A Trailing Stop Loss moves automatically as the token price increases. The Trailing Value (%) represents the distance between the current price and where the stop loss is set. As the token price rises, the stop loss moves up with it, always maintaining that distance. If the price drops enough to hit the trailing level, the order triggers and closes the position automatically.

Profit/Loss %

Set take profit or stop loss. • 📈 **Take Profit:** Use positive values (e.g., +100% for 2x)

• 📉 **Stop Loss:** Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)

Fixed Mcap

Set the target market cap at which you’d like Bloom to sell.

Mcap Variation

Set the market cap increase or decrease threshold at which you’d like Bloom to sell. Bloom will execute the sale only when the market cap change matches your specified value.

Sell at

This button adapts based on your selected selling method (Profit/Loss %, Fixed MCap, MCap Variation), allowing you to set your preferred value accordingly.

Enter your target value:

• Take Profit: e.g. 50%, 150%.

• Stop Loss: e.g. -20%, -50%.

Examples:

• Profit %: 100%: your holdings will be sold at 2x.

• Loss %: -50%: your holdings will be sold when the price drops by 50%.

Notes:

• Only one % value (TP or SL) per limit order.

Sell Amount

Set the target amount to sell as a percentage.

Please enter your desired sell amount:

Example:

• For a sell of 10%, enter 10

Slippage

Set the slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Sell Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

High Impact (Expert only)

Enables trades that require higher price impact than usual. Use this if you’re buying large amounts of SOL in low-liquidity pools. ⚠️ **Expert users only:** using this when it’s not needed can route the sale through suboptimal pools or cause bad slippage.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

Please enter your desired priority fee:

Example:

• For a priority fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Back

Return to the previous menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

Once the orders are created, you can edit them by selecting the target order or cancel them by clicking `🗑️ Delete Order` in the dedicated menu, as shown below.

Max Buy Count

Specify how many of the target account’s posted contracts you want the bot to purchase. e._g. • If you enter 1, Bloom will only buy the first contract posted. • If you enter 2, Bloom will buy both the first and the second contracts posted._

_If you change target account, the parameter won't reset._

Please enter your desired number of tokens to trade or enter -1 to disable:

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

🟢: When enabled, Bloom automatically buys contracts posted in a post reply according to your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Social Bio Update

🟢: When enabled, Bloom automatically buys contracts posted in bio the moment the bio changes according to your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Social Repost

🟢: When enabled, Bloom automatically buys contracts posted in the original reposted post, following your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Social OCR

🟢: When enabled, Bloom uses OCR to automatically buy contracts from images.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

• Use K for thousands, M for millions, B for billions

Trailing

A Trailing Stop Loss moves automatically as the token price increases. The Trailing Value (%) represents the distance between the current price and where the stop loss is set. As the token price rises, the stop loss moves up with it, always maintaining that distance. If the price drops enough to hit the trailing level, the order triggers and closes the position automatically.

Fixed Mcap

Set the target market cap at which you’d like Bloom to sell.

• 📉 **Stop Loss:** Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)

Mcap Variation

Set the market cap increase or decrease threshold at which you’d like Bloom to sell. Bloom will execute the sale only when the market cap change matches your specified value.

Sell at

This button adapts based on your selected selling method (Profit/Loss %, Fixed MCap, MCap Variation), allowing you to set your preferred value accordingly.

Enter your target value:

• Take Profit: e.g. 50%, 150%.

• Stop Loss: e.g. -20%, -50%.

Examples:

• Profit %: 100%: your holdings will be sold at 2x.

• Loss %: -50%: your holdings will be sold when the price drops by 50%.

Notes:

• Only one % value (TP or SL) per limit order.

Sell Amount

Set the target amount to sell as a percentage.

Please enter your desired sell amount:

Example:

• For a sell of 10%, enter 10

Sell Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

Please enter your desired priority fee:

Example:

• For a priority fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Slippage

Set the slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Auto Orders


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Copy | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good afternoon

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

Copy-Trading allows you to mirror a target trader’s wallet by entering their address. Each copy-trading task can be fully customized through our settings to suit your specific needs.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/copy#before-you-start)

Before you start

✅ Ensure you set a [Copy-Trading Default Wallet](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/wallets)
.

🕒 Please wait 30 seconds after each change for it to take effect.

📝 **Changing your default wallet?** Remember to remake your tasks to use the new wallet for future transactions.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/copy#tipping-suggestios)

Tipping Suggestions

The higher the Bundle Tip (JITO), the lower the slippage should be. Conversely, the lower the Bundle Tip (JITO), the higher the slippage should be.

Without a JITO tip, the risk of getting MEV increases significantly.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot/copy#blacklist-info)

Blacklist Info

Adding an address to the blacklist applies across all your copy-trading configurations. This prevents any trades involving those addresses, regardless of the target wallet.

Please enter your desired max trades per token or enter -1 to disable:

Resets the number of times your configuration has bought that token.

First Interaction

🟢: If enabled, it will trigger trades only when the trader you’re copy-trading interacts with the token for the first time 🔴: If disabled, the bot will not consider whether the trader has previously interacted with the token or not.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Sell Only Copied Buys

Sells trigger only for tokens bought via copytrading, excluding Spot, Twitter and AFK purchases.

Platforms

Choose the platform to activate the AFK task on. After selection, set up the task, and AFK Mode will be enabled on all chosen platforms.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FBlrHQfg9m5m66xUEopMs%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252012.38.29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D480f573e-e724-4a28-a38b-ace0d2b7e352&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8428cb84&sv=2)

Max Buy

Set the maximum amount you’re willing to buy, regardless of the amount purchased by the target wallet. _**Max Buy applies to each transaction.**_

Please enter your desired number of tokens to trade or enter -1 to disable:

Min Trigger Buy

Set the minimum SOL amount purchased by the target wallet required for your transaction to be executed.

Please enter your desired min trigger buy amount in SOL or enter -1 to disable:

Set the maximum SOL amount purchased by the target wallet required for your transaction to be executed.

Please enter your desired max trigger buy amount in SOL or enter -1 to disable:

Set the minimum market cap you are willing to buy at.

Please enter your desired market cap or enter -1 to disable:

• Use K for thousands, M for millions, B for billions

• $12 million: Enter 12M or 12000000

• $500,000: Enter 500K or 0.5M

Max MCap

Set the maximum market cap you are willing to buy at.

Please enter your desired market cap or enter -1 to disable:

• Use K for thousands, M for millions, B for billions

Examples:

• $12 million: Enter 12M or 12000000

• $500,000: Enter 500K or 0.5M

Min Token Age

• Set the minimum amount of time passed since the token was created. • For Pump.fun migrated coins, the time is calculated from the moment they bonded. _Note: Some older tokens may not work properly with this filter._

Please enter the token age or enter -1 to disable:

📝 Format examples:

• 1H = 1 hour

• 30M = 30 minutes

• 1D = 1 day

• 60 = 60 seconds

Supported units:

• H = hours

• M = minutes

• D = days

• Direct number = seconds

Max Token Age

• Set the maximum amount of time passed since the token was created. • For Pump.fun migrated coins, the time is calculated from the moment they bonded. _Note: Some older tokens may not work properly with this filter._

Please enter the token age or enter -1 to disable:

📝 Format examples:

• 1H = 1 hour

• 30M = 30 minutes

• 1D = 1 day

• 60 = 60 seconds

Supported units:

• H = hours

• M = minutes

• D = days

• Direct number = seconds

Reverse Mode

Purchases are triggered exclusively when the target wallet sells.

_Buy transactions from the target wallet are ignored._ _**Reverse Mode Min Sell:**_ Set the minimum percentage the target wallet must sell to trigger the task.

Skip Deploys

Skip a target wallet’s buy when the token deployer is the target wallet itself.

Follow Sells

Choose whether to sell when the target wallet sells.

_When enabled, the bot will mirror the selling percentage of the trader - for example, if they sell 50% of their position, the bot will also sell 50% of your position_

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Only Once

Buy the coin only once, even if the target wallet makes multiple purchases. _If you’re using multiple wallets, ensure it’s enabled for each one._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Exact

Buy the same SOL amount as the target wallet.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy %

Buy a percentage of the amount the target wallet buys. _You can set it above 100% to purchase more than the target wallet (eg. 130% buys an additional 30% of the amount purchased by the target wallet)._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Fixed

Buy a fixed SOL amount, regardless of the target wallet’s amount.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Fee

Set the transaction fee for buying.

Example:

• For a priority fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Sell Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

Please enter your desired priority fee:

Example:

• For a priority fee of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Buy Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Sell Slippage

Set the sell slippage percentage.

Please enter your desired slippage:

Example:

• For a slippage of 10%, enter 10

Buy Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Sell Protection

Toggle MEV protection (enabled/disabled) to prevent your transaction from being sandwiched. The fastest processor is automatically used.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Auto Tip

If enabled, it automatically selects the Jito-suggested tip.

_Priority fees are set to a fixed amount since the tip is what matters for Jito Blocks._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Tip

Set the target buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Sell Tip

Set the target sell tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

Please enter your desired tip:

Example:

• For a tip of 0.01 SOL, enter 0.01

Copy-Trading Limit Orders


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Click on `🤖 Copy Trade` in the home menu or use the `/copy` command.
    
*   Click `🆕 Add New Config` or and already existing config.
    
*   Click `📈 Limit Orders`. ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FNSDySM5meLzinN9K435O%252Flmcp.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17bfef13-60c7-4bd7-8612-0d26190df62f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=52459fe5&sv=2)
    
*   Click `🆕 Create Limit Order`. ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FtYBrE2ULAex8SXxTSTrD%252Flmsn2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9d03298b-9dee-4fee-8975-b8b73d46d1c1&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=105c3420&sv=2)
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F4qar7idmeU5Hx1bTyEwg%252FScreenshot%25202024-12-17%2520alle%252019.46.16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4010328b-c175-4fc3-803c-aa1b411bf3c5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8e6b48b&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Sell Amount

Enter the % to be sold for the Take Profit and Stop Loss.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Profit/Loss

Set take profit or stop loss. • 📈 **Take Profit:** Use positive values (e.g., +100% for 2x)

• 📉 **Stop Loss:** Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Bundle Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Dev Sell

Choose whether to automatically sell the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. If enabled, the bot will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Back

Return to the previous menu.

Refresh

Refresh the menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

Once the orders are created, you can edit them by selecting the target order or cancel them by clicking `🗑️ Delete Order` in the dedicated menu, as shown below.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

.

    task by entering the token address.

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

`Please enter your desired amount: (SOL, %, hours)`

Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

`Please enter your desired amount: (SOL, %, hours)`

Dev Sell

Choose whether to automatically sell the specified amount if the Dev sells any of their tokens. If enabled, the bot will ignore the set profit/loss percentage and only trigger a sale when the Dev sells.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Choose to create the order based on market cap.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/limit-orders/limit-sell#take-profit)

Take Profit


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set multiple Take Profits, create separate orders with different market caps/prices and percentages aligned with your goals and strategy.

Follow the steps below to set up your take profit strategy.

1.  Enter the Take Profit percentage with `+` in front of the value (eg. +50) in `💰 Market Cap` or `💰 Price` according to your target.
    
2.  Setup the order as a regular Limit Sell one.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/limit-orders/limit-sell#stop-loss)

Stop Loss


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Follow the steps below to set up your stop loss strategy.

1.  Enter the Stop Loss percentage with `-` in front of the value (eg. -50) in `💰 Market Cap` or `💰 Price` according to your target.
    
2.  Setup the order as a regular Limit Sell one.
    

Last updated 9 months ago

*   [Create a Sell Order](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/limit-orders/limit-sell#create-a-sell-order)
    
*   [Take Profit](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/limit-orders/limit-sell#take-profit)
    
*   [Stop Loss](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/limit-orders/limit-sell#stop-loss)

# Limit Orders | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good afternoon

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

Limit orders allow you to set a specific price at which you want to buy or sell a cryptocurrency. Unlike market orders that execute immediately at the current price, limit orders only trigger when the market reaches your desired price or market cap.

Additionally, you can customize your order with multiple parameters, ensuring your trade is tailored to your strategy.

[https://youtu.be/rS9qzysbTrsyoutu.be](https://youtu.be/rS9qzysbTrs)

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/limit-orders/limit-buy)

# Copy | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good evening

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

Copy-Trading allows you to mirror a target trader’s wallet by entering their address. Each copy-trading task can be fully customized through our settings to suit your specific needs.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/copy#before-you-start)

Before you start

✅ Ensure you set a [Copy-Trading Default Wallet](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/wallets#wallet-settings)
.

🕒 Please wait 30 seconds after each change for it to take effect.

📝 **Changing your default wallet?** Remember to remake your tasks to use the new wallet for future transactions.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/copy#tipping-suggestios)

Tipping Suggestios

The higher the Bundle Tip (JITO), the lower the slippage should be. Conversely, the lower the Bundle Tip (JITO), the higher the slippage should be.

Without a JITO tip, the risk of getting MEV increases significantly.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/copy#blacklist-info)

Blacklist Info

Adding an address to the blacklist applies across all your copy-trading configurations. This prevents any trades involving those addresses, regardless of the target wallet.

[https://youtu.be/AEMzsTx6PaMyoutu.be](https://youtu.be/AEMzsTx6PaM)

* * *

Access the copy-tading menu directly by using the `/copy` command or from the `/start` menu.

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/copy#setup)

Setup


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F7RwXfcpaJOdgui19lwT1%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-10%2520alle%252018.05.29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1caa6c68-5f37-48ae-86fb-1b3873808991&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8f218c8a&sv=2)

🔴 – The copy-trading profile is **inactive**.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FISdSLjP4kIVvpgesP2iv%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-10%2520alle%252018.05.35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54347e2a-53e4-4070-95dd-9f2ee68c4226&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db7feb6a&sv=2)

Max Fee

Set the maximum fee you’re willing to pay for a successful transaction. The fee charged will range between your Min Fee and Max Fee amounts.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FIGqDYxeSfo3B3Z5BcBRh%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-18%2520alle%252015.25.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54c17f5a-a20d-440f-b2cc-0fb3b931bcac&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d2cf9c&sv=2)

Min Fee

Set the minimum fee amount you’d be charged if the transaction fails. You won’t be charged more than this value in case of failure.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F7nDwyQRfJmZbkk7w31ee%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-18%2520alle%252015.25.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcfeac385-d46b-48c8-b94a-807d1de12f06&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3da6dcdd&sv=2)

Min Amount Out

Set the minimum number of tokens you want to receive.

`Please enter the minimum amount out. You can enter a number with K/M suffixes or enter -1 to disable:`

Limit Orders

[Check out the dedicated guide.](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/sniper-limit-orders)

Delete Task

Delete sniper task.

Back

Return to the previous menu.

Refresh

Refresh the menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

How to Buy


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FLxLdPPlXNAkqrYilqUTb%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-28%2520alle%252015.29.05.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc778f0c6-4bc2-4f5a-b820-61e2cbf237a9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1745ff89&sv=2)

PnL pic to be shared.

Hide Position

Hide the current position.

Auto Tip

If enabled, it automatically selects the Jito-suggested tip, ranging from 0.015 to 0.15.

_Priority fees are set to a fixed amount since the tip is what matters for Jito Blocks._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

MEV Protect

The fastest processor is automatically used to ensure maximum transaction success, whether MEV Protection is ON or OFF. ❓ [FAQs](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#mev-protect-and-processors)

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Multi-Wallet Buy


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To buy with multiple wallets, you need to activate them first. Follow these steps:

1.  Click `💰 Active Wallets`.
    
2.  Activate or deactivate wallets based on your preferences. ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F95B5VPnW1nxxUyb8KJXU%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-06%2520alle%252017.20.27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df81a14e7-6a8b-4810-9c39-9082eb4a9bd5&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1c88da67&sv=2)
    
3.  Once done, click `⬅️ Back` to return to the buy menu.

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/limit-orders/active-orders#retrive-active-orders)

Retrive Active Orders


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Follow the steps below to view all your active orders across all the coins:

1.  Run `/orders` command.
    
2.  You will be prompted to the following menu, where you can view the coins with active orders. ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FjJ47SUfsdzz6P989c8My%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-16%2520alle%252013.29.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a778e9f-ca6e-46ad-a050-0c3bf01c0802&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=249392b0&sv=2)
    
3.  Select the coin for which you want to open the orders menu. The menu shown in the image below will appear. ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FtPeKLASast9rgXSGG14x%252Flo1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0fc83ca1-8dec-4408-baff-7f22226732ef&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ad881435&sv=2)
    
4.  This menu provides an overview of all your current open orders for the selected coin. By clicking `🗑️ Delete Order`, you can cancel the corresponding order displayed on the left. _eg._ ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FXhEroZEPFFmNt9FNBjDe%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-16%2520alle%252013.41.01.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5283f7a9-f460-46f9-88bc-4afadf9670ea&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=105e4f5d&sv=2) _By clicking_ `_🗑️ Delete Order_`_, you will delete the_ `_🤑 Limit Buy (#1)_` _order._

# Slippage | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good night

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

Slippage is the difference between the expected price of a trade and the actual price at which the trade is executed. It typically occurs during periods of high volatility or low liquidity. Generally, the higher it is, the faster your transaction is but the higher are the chances of getting your transaction sandwiched.

* * *

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F0mgUaarqzM9VbpSqAaFV%252FScreenshot%25202024-12-08%2520alle%252023.39.33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dec913e18-2cfb-4b80-97b6-9555b911716e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d02c532&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Buy Slip

Set the buy slippage percentage.

`Please enter your desired buy slippage amount in %:`

Sell Slip

Set the sell slippage percentage.

`Please enter your desired buy slippage amount in %:`

AI Based on your context

Send

**Always keep your address locked when not making updates. It’s one of the most effective measures to protect your funds from unauthorized access or malicious attacks.**

[https://youtu.be/vj4dnF1oqK0youtu.be](https://youtu.be/vj4dnF1oqK0)

* * *

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F2CP550QaahzN07i7LFlU%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3be49d83-5845-4926-8fc9-1b80f88f8a1c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=38fa139d&sv=2)

Action

Response

50%, 100%

Preset percentage of SOL you want to withdraw (e.g., 50% withdraws half your funds).

X SOL

Edit the amount of SOL you wish to withdraw.

Set Address

Set the address to receive your funds.

`Please enter your Solana withdrawal address:`

Lock Address

Lock your address to prevent changes. This safety measure ensures that no malicious party can modify the address or withdraw your funds for 24 hours unlocking it.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FbPZJXWwAcfj7g1Bhy4q0%252FScreenshot%25202024-11-18%2520alle%252021.18.31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dda901c40-5b33-4045-bbe6-1c6b4576e30f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5d53ccb1&sv=2)

Unlock Address

Unlock your address if you need to make changes. A 24-hour security cooldown will be applied before any modifications are allowed.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FJJzR01mYXeGTBoJWOrh9%252FScreenshot%25202024-11-18%2520alle%252021.09.51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46fb1a56-557c-4e23-99e1-afa07d902530&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9df323eb&sv=2)

Back

Return to the previous page.

Refresh

Refresh the menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/withdraw#locking-unlocking-withdraw-address)

Locking/Unlocking Withdraw Address


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Protecting your funds is our top priority, and we’ve implemented a safety feature to help safeguard your wallet: Address Locking.

🔒 Why locking your address?[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/withdraw#why-locking-your-address)

Locking your address ensures it cannot be changed while locked, making it impossible for anyone—including potential attackers—to replace it and withdraw your funds. This is a critical layer of security, especially in case of a malicious attack or if your wallet becomes compromised.

🔓 Unlocking your address[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/withdraw#unlocking-your-address)

If you need to make changes to your address, you must first unlock it. Once unlocked, a 24-hour security cooldown begins, ensuring that no changes can be made during this time. This delay provides a buffer to detect and prevent unauthorized attempts.

Last updated 8 months ago

---

# Afk | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good morning

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

AFK Mode allows you to automate your trades while you’re away. By setting up key parameters and configurations, the bot will automatically execute buy and sell orders on your behalf based on your inputs.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/afk#benefits-of-afk-mode)

**Benefits of AFK Mode**

1.  **Trade effortlessly**: You can potentially make profits even while you’re away, as the bot manages trades for you.
    
2.  **Tailored settings**: You control how the bot operates with various parameters, ensuring it aligns with your trading strategy.
    
3.  **Multi-Testing:** With AFK Mode, you can run multiple trading setups simultaneously to find the most profitable and reliable strategy.
    

Setting up AFK Mode properly requires time and effort. A well-configured setup can maximize your chances of success, but it’s essential to carefully adjust the parameters to fit your goals.

[https://youtu.be/qcTUKMlv3LEyoutu.be](https://youtu.be/qcTUKMlv3LE)

* * *

Access `💤 AFK Mode` easily from the home menu or by using the `/afk` command.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FmqFxGqVFNhf7JrndECEO%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9bae0acf-462a-440d-99ef-07ec27f13051&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ab7d964&sv=2)

# Degen Mode | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good night

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

Degen Mode instantly buys a token as soon as its contract address is entered in Telegram, without asking for additional details. Once typed, it will attempt to purchase based on your settings, regardless of your balance.

*   When enabled, Degen Mode will attempt to **buy immediately as soon as the token address is entered**, even before the token menu appears. It will try to execute the purchase regardless of the wallet balance.
    
*   Once the token is sold, it won’t attempt to rebuy, even if auto-buy is enabled.
    

**🟢 ON –** Automatically buy a coin when the coin address is pasted. 🔴 **OFF –** Manually start buy when the coin address is pasted.

[https://youtu.be/hjqBvCBXZtIyoutu.be](https://youtu.be/hjqBvCBXZtI)

* * *

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F0Ky6DnyX74lGE0RdXmu7%252FScreenshot%25202024-12-25%2520alle%252018.29.06.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3df4a5f-2c12-4196-bd6b-4068d1e09b8b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=68e0d96a&sv=2)

*   Click `🟢🔴 Degen Mode`.

Wallets Menu


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F4REVc3UMv4hhqIfBznJV%252FScreenshot%25202024-12-02%2520alle%252023.33.05.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56756d93-0b89-4c65-b6d5-5cdf05820162&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=182e6467&sv=2)

From the wallets menu, you can create, import, manage, and set a default wallet.

Button

Action

Response

Create Wallet

Create a new wallet. Get the private key and address. Make sure to copy and save the private key!

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FzVhTYK82GVyeFyVSj11t%252F123.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f63bbde-dfe1-4ac6-9327-c6e9442ffb6b&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=968ddb80&sv=2)

Import Wallet

Import an existing wallet.

Wallet Settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FZEYeQOFaQ9Yg7e2lME06%252FScreenshot%25202024-11-28%2520alle%252023.05.06.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e5341b1-58b8-408c-8f3f-876c7d3a4f24&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=50b88461&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Default

Set wallet as default. _To change the default wallet, set the new one as default._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Copy

Set wallet as default for copy-trading. _Change by selecting a new one._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Sniper

Activate as sniper wallet.

_Note: Multiple wallets can be activated._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Spot

Enable as spot buy and sell wallet.

_Note: Multiple wallets can be activated._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Set Name

Rename wallet.

`Please enter your desired wallet name:`

Delete

Delete wallet.

Below are a few additional settings—like MEV Protect and Slippage—which you can find explained in our [FAQs](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs)
.

Button

Action

Response

MEV Protect _(_Spot Buy and Spot Sell)

The fastest processor is automatically used to ensure maximum transaction success, whether MEV Protection is ON or OFF. ❓ [FAQs](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/miscellaneous/faqs#mev-protect-and-processors)

🟢: Jito 🔴: Select processor (Buy, Sell)

Expert Mode

If active, It reduces the amount of information displayed for the coin in the Buy/Sell and Positions menus.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Private PNL

When enabled, the PnL card will hide the following amounts: Profit/Loss value and percentage.

🇺🇸 🇨🇳 🇷🇺

Switch language: • English • Chinese • Russian

Back

Return to the previous page.

Close

Close the current menu.

# Sniper Limit Orders | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good evening

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/sniper-limit-orders#sniper-limit-orders)

Sniper Limit Orders


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Run the `/settings` command.
    
2.  Click `🎯 Sniper Presets`.
    
3.  Click `📈 Limit Orders`. ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fvi1tdkBB2L3IgeNcRT0m%252Flmsn1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddbd9e07d-8819-4896-8418-24101b34d10e&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=33402e47&sv=2)
    
4.  Click `🆕 Create Limit Order`. ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F5sPPVGu6k7Kan7eKiHSU%252Flmsn2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74d37696-08a1-46d9-aa3d-66d2cbfa7e11&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9e68e929&sv=2)
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FxwBxlDWxDa5w2XNxXNrw%252FScreenshot%25202024-11-02%2520alle%252017.38.58.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db6bd9a57-5631-4c90-b99d-0796995f22c4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=96631403&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Sell Amount

Enter the % to be sold for the Take Profit and Stop Loss.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Profit/Loss

Set take profit or stop loss. • 📈 **Take Profit:** Use positive values (e.g., +100% for 2x)

• 📉 **Stop Loss:** Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Bundle Tip

Set the buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Back

Return to the previous menu.

Refresh

Refresh the menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

Once the orders are created, you can edit them by selecting the target order or cancel them by clicking `🗑️ Delete Order` in the dedicated menu, as shown below.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FPnYU0w7yMznKDOcEcmZd%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-31%2520alle%252017.54.56.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87552933-0fcc-41b4-b618-ea8d93bef52e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0d9c5a0&sv=2)

Last updated 9 months ago

# Afk Presets | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good night

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

AFK Presets allow you to set the default configurations used when running an AFK Mode task.

* * *

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fsm85EhUSlMNkGF7qyHxG%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-07%2520alle%252013.59.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc21a1c6-cf85-4b31-a13e-1ce9a824e610&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f756458f&sv=2)

*   Click `💤 AFK Presets`.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FKpYYE0gJ7wpjz5oMTlW2%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-07%2520alle%252014.00.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ab71f48-ed8a-4e94-86e4-3d54b1357efb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9837690a&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Max Traded Token

Set the maximum number of coins the bot will purchase according to your current configuration.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Buy

Choose the SOL amount to buy.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Fee

Set the transaction fee for buying.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Mev Protect

The fastest processor is automatically used to ensure maximum transaction success, whether MEV Protection is ON or OFF.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Tip

Set the target buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Twitter Tweet

When enabled, Bloom automatically buys tweeted contracts according to your settings. _(Including quoted retweets where the contract is taken from the quoted text)._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Twitter Reply

When enabled, Bloom automatically buys contracts posted in a Tweet reply according to your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Twitter Bio Update

When enabled, Bloom automatically buys contracts posted in bio the moment the bio changes according to your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Twitter Retweet

When enabled, Bloom automatically buys contracts posted in the original retweeted post, following your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Pre Bonding PF

When enabled, Bloom automatically buys PumpFun contracts according to your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Other/After Bonding

When enabled, Bloom automatically buys non-PumpFun tokens (e.g., Orca, Raydium) according to your settings.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Min Market Cap

Set the minimum market cap you are willing to buy at.

`Please enter your desired market cap (eg: 12M / 1K / 10000):`

Max Market Cap

Set the maximum market cap you are willing to buy at.

`Please enter your desired market cap (eg: 12M / 1K / 10000):`

Min Token Age

• Set the minimum amount of time passed since the token was created. • For Pump.fun migrated coins, the time is calculated from the moment they bonded.

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/settings/presets/afk-presets#auto-orders)

Auto Orders


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Auto orders are limit orders automatically created after you buy a coin. They trigger based on your settings and don’t require you to start them manually once created.

After creation, the task will automatically start post-buy. Make sure to delete it if you don't want it to run.

*   Click `📈 Limit Orders`.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FK1Fv1gnxZtsr59A273xA%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-07%2520alle%252014.27.37.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd079dab5-fb57-448e-a4e8-815e282b8e15&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=33c7b776&sv=2)

*   Click `🆕 Create Limit Order`.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FiJ2yM7FjOg5bCfjU1ShW%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-06%2520alle%252018.46.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D840abc62-e00a-4303-9aaf-1879b8af1551&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=571af960&sv=2)

# Normal Mode | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good afternoon

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

Sniping is crucial for fast trades during Pumpfun migrations, Moonshot migrations, and Raydium new liquidity pools. It helps you send transactions quickly, outpacing the competition when timing is critical.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/normal-mode#before-you-start)

Before you start

Ensure you set a [Sniper Default Wallet](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/wallets#wallet-settings)
.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/normal-mode#id-3-pending-transactions)

3 Pending Transactions

Don’t be alarmed if you see three pending messages when you initiate a sniper task. The sniper sends one transaction from each of our servers, but only one of the three pending transactions will be confirmed.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/normal-mode#mev-protect)

MEV Protect

On Normal Mode **MEV Protect is enabled** by default.

### 

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/normal-mode#tipping-suggestios)

Tipping Suggestios

The higher the Buy or Sell Tip (Processors), the lower the slippage should be. Conversely, the lower the Buy or Sell Tip (Processors), the higher the slippage should be.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/normal-mode#interactive-tutorial)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/normal-mode#sell-reverse-sniper)

Sell (Reverse Sniper)


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Reverse sniping is used when you've already bought a coin un Pump.fun and want to sell it instantly when it migrates to Raydium. It works like sniping, but instead of buying, you’re selling.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FhjgwM5LNclwCP2oECR0E%252FScreenshot%25202025-01-09%2520alle%252017.41.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db73af4a2-9678-42d7-b029-0e5e50ad3e1b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c50a7864&sv=2)

1.  To reverse snipe, either run the `/sniper` command or click `🎯 LP Sniper` in the main menu.
    
2.  Tap `🎯 Create Task` or click on an already existing one.
    
3.  Click `🔄 Switch to Sell`.
    
4.  Set it up
    

Button

Action

Action

Switch to Buy

[Refer to the dedicated guide.](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana-bot/sniper#create-sniper-task)

Choose the % to sell.

Add the Sniper Wallets by clicking `🎯 Sniper Wallets`. ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252F0SNM0sUeMrXwFeFtlnwA%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b3bb9ab-71d6-42bf-876a-e978addb9904&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b945c9d&sv=2)
    
3.  Tap on the wallet you would like to activate for sniping. ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FiD2Ku5LdOuF1pQ6Hlx1h%252FScreenshot%25202024-11-30%2520alle%252016.52.54.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad469243-8f90-4b0c-91ba-6e24bb6155cc&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=13e4ae15&sv=2)

# Copy Presets | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

##### Good evening

I'm here to help you with the docs.

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

Copy Presets allow you to set the default configurations used when running a copy-trading task.

* * *

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FoLbpAqeJGEJuYd42YMan%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-07%2520alle%252013.59.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc333c3ac-a552-4769-be91-892cd927f355&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=823df78&sv=2)

*   Click `🤖 Copy Presets`.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FB4tydxmadqFycCgxwPpj%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-10%2520alle%252018.07.15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57d26e4b-dbc1-49fd-8980-ac4b9b7aee4a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=267fd000&sv=2)

Button

Action

Response

Max Traded Token

Set the maximum number of coins the bot will purchase according to your current configuration.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

First Interaction

🟢: If enabled, it will trigger trades only when the trader you’re copy-trading interacts with the token for the first time 🔴: If disabled, the bot will not consider whether the trader has previously interacted with the token or not.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Max Buy

Set the maximum amount you’re willing to buy, regardless of the amount purchased by the target wallet. _**Max Buy applies to each transaction.**_

`Please enter your desired max buy amount in SOL:`

Buy Exact

Buy the same SOL amount as the target wallet.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy %

Buy a percentage of the amount the target wallet buys. _You can set it above 100% to purchase more than the target wallet (eg. 130% buys an additional 30% of the amount purchased by the target wallet)._

`Buy Amount: Set it to the desired percentage to turn it on`

Buy Fixed

Buy a fixed SOL amount, regardless of the target wallet’s amount.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Min MCap

Set the minimum market cap you are willing to buy at.

`Please enter your desired market cap (eg: 12M / 1K / 10000):`

Max MCap

Set the maximum market cap you are willing to buy at.

`Please enter your desired market cap (eg: 12M / 1K / 10000):`

Follow Sell

Choose whether to sell when the target wallet sells.

_When enabled, the bot will mirror the selling percentage of the trader - for example, if they sell 50% of their position, the bot will also sell 50% of your position_

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Only Once

Buy the coin only once, even if the target wallet makes multiple purchases. _If you’re using multiple wallets, ensure it’s turned ON for each one._

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Fee

Set the transaction fee for buying.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Sell Fee

Set the transaction fee for selling.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Buy Slippage

Set the buy slippage percentage.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Sell Slippage

Set the sell slippage percentage.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Mev Protect

The fastest processor is automatically used to ensure maximum transaction success, whether MEV Protection is ON or OFF.

🟢: Active

🔴: Inactive

Buy Tip

Set the target buy tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Sell Tip

Set the target sell tip fee to prioritize the inclusion of your transaction in the next block.

`Please enter your desired amount:`

Limit Orders

[Refer to the dedicated guide.](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/copy/copy-limit-orders)

⬅️Back

Return to the previous page.

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/settings/presets/copy-presets#auto-orders)

Auto Orders


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Auto orders are limit orders automatically created after you buy a coin. They trigger based on your settings and don’t require you to start them manually once created.

After creation, the task will automatically start post-buy. Make sure to delete it if you don't want it to run.

*   Click `📈 Limit Orders`.
    

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FivRLJHgvsjMFbJ87xdYt%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-07%2520alle%252014.30.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5cfe41b0-1fec-43a1-84aa-fa0132f5feab&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=214dcc70&sv=2)

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fo2s6fTl90yXDHGPFJ15A%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-06%2520alle%252018.48.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D148b32d1-d95f-48a7-bade-5c61b0f44e97&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e65be111&sv=2)

# PRO Mode | Solana | Bloom

GitBook Assistant

GitBook Assistant

Working...Thinking...

GitBook Assistant

##### Good evening

I'm here to help you with the docs.

What is this page about?What should I read next?Can you give an example?

Ctrli

AI Based on your context

Send

PRO Mode is a custom-developed feature designed to significantly enhance sniping performance. While we can’t disclose all the details, here’s what you need to know:

1.  The **fastest processor** is automatically use to maximize the success of your snipe.
    
2.  **Successful Transactions:** You’ll never spend more than your Max Fee.
    
3.  **Failed Transactions:** The amount you pay won’t exceed your Min Fee amount.
    
4.  It’s recommended to set your Max Priority Fee lower than your Max Total Fee for optimal cost management.
    
5.  No MEV Protection – If you require MEV protection, switch to Normal Mode.
    
6.  To create a PRO account, your wallet **must have balance**. Wallets with zero balance cannot be upgraded to PRO.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.bloombot.app/solana/solana-bot-1.0-old/sniper/pro-mode#interactive-tutorial)

Interactive Tutorial


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

1.  To access the sniper menu, either run the `/sniper` command or click `🎯 LP Sniper` in the main menu.
    
    ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FclcHDUomJViTd4QS9Wcu%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D079453e6-29ca-42e5-a60d-c6fc790208d4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9398eac0&sv=2)
    
2.  Access the pro account menu by clicking `🎯 Pro Accounts`.
    
3.  Turn a sniper account PRO by clicking `⚡️ Create PRO`.
    
    ![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FCFyUoI9DTcQMCDvLzE8K%252Fpro%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e45c765-e4b2-4d65-b499-5c7eca69053f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a2a709a3&sv=2)
    
4.  Update the status by clicking `🔄 Refresh`.

Sell (Reverse Sniper)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Reverse sniping is used when you've already bought a coin un Pump.fun and want to sell it instantly when it migrates to Raydium. It works like sniping, but instead of buying, you’re selling.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252Fz8b6eXAnxXFMfxx3KPdA%252FScreenshot%25202025-01-09%2520alle%252017.43.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5f9b680-3c35-4064-b51f-3d01685bb2cc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cb4e5a38&sv=2)

1.  To reverse snipe, either run the `/sniper` command or click `🎯 LP Sniper` in the main menu.
    
2.  Tap `🎯 Create Task` or click on an already existing one.
    
3.  Click `🔄 Switch to Sell`.
    
4.  Set it up

Sell Amount

• 📉 **Stop Loss:** Use negative values (e.g., -50% for half)

Refresh

Refresh the menu.

Close

Close the current menu.

Once the orders are created, you can edit them by selecting the target order or cancel them by clicking `🗑️ Delete Order` in the dedicated menu, as shown below.

![](https://docs.bloombot.app/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4108356913-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FtLeahxvohQr3fYBgeulA%252Fuploads%252FPnYU0w7yMznKDOcEcmZd%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-31%2520alle%252017.54.56.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87552933-0fcc-41b4-b618-ea8d93bef52e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b0d9c5a0&sv=2)
